      ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        // Update glitch animation
        slices.forEach(slice => {
          slice.glitchTime--;
          
          if (slice.glitchTime <= 0) {
            // New glitch
            if (Math.random() < 0.1) {
              slice.glitchTime = Math.floor(Math.random() * 20) + 5;
              slice.glitchDuration = slice.glitchTime;
              slice.offset = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 40;
            }
          }
          
          // Draw slice
          ctx.save();
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.rect(0, slice.y, width, sliceHeight);
          ctx.clip();
          
          // RGB shift
          if (slice.glitchTime > 0) {
            const progress = slice.glitchTime / slice.glitchDuration;
            
            // Red channel
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgb(255, 0, 0)';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2 + slice.offset * progress, height / 2);
            
            // Green channel
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgb(0, 255, 0)';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
            
            // Blue channel
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgb(0, 0, 255)';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2 - slice.offset * progress, height / 2);
          } else {
            // Normal rendering
            ctx.fillStyle = 'white';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
          }
          
          ctx.restore();
        });
        
        // Random noise
        if (Math.random() < 0.1) {
          for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
            const noiseX = Math.random() * width;
            const noiseY = Math.random() * height;
            const noiseW = Math.random() * 40 + 10;
            const noiseH = Math.random() * 5 + 2;
            
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.5)';
            ctx.fillRect(noiseX, noiseY, noiseW, noiseH);
          }
        }
      } else {
        // Static display
        ctx.fillStyle = 'white';
        ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Morphing text effect
  const renderMorphingText = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Text to morph between
    const words = ['MORPH', 'TEXT', 'EFFECT'];
    let currentIndex = 0;
    let nextIndex = 1;
    let progress = 0;
    const morphSpeed = 0.01;
    
    // Generate points for text
    const generateTextPoints = (text) => {
      ctx.font = 'bold 80px Arial';
      ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
      
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
      
      const imageData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
      const pixels = imageData.data;
      const points = [];
      
      // Sample points
      const sampleSize = 3;
      for (let y = 0; y < height; y += sampleSize) {
        for (let x = 0; x < width; x += sampleSize) {
          const i = (y * width + x) * 4;
          if (pixels[i + 3] > 128) { // If pixel is opaque enough
            points.push({
              x,
              y,
              originX: x,
              originY: y
            });
          }
        }
      }
      
      return points;
    };
    
    let sourcePoints = generateTextPoints(words[currentIndex]);
    let targetPoints = generateTextPoints(words[nextIndex]);
    
    // Match point counts
    const matchPointCounts = () => {
      // Make source and target have the same number of points
      const minPoints = Math.min(sourcePoints.length, targetPoints.length);
      const maxPoints = Math.max(sourcePoints.length, targetPoints.length);
      
      if (sourcePoints.length < targetPoints.length) {
        // Add random existing points to source
        for (let i = minPoints; i < maxPoints; i++) {
          const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * minPoints);
          sourcePoints.push({ ...sourcePoints[randomIndex] });
        }
      } else if (targetPoints.length < sourcePoints.length) {
        // Add random existing points to target
        for (let i = minPoints; i < maxPoints; i++) {
          const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * minPoints);
          targetPoints.push({ ...targetPoints[randomIndex] });
        }
      }
    };
    
    matchPointCounts();
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        // Update progress
        progress += morphSpeed;
        
        if (progress >= 1) {
          progress = 0;
          currentIndex = nextIndex;
          nextIndex = (nextIndex + 1) % words.length;
          sourcePoints = targetPoints;
          targetPoints = generateTextPoints(words[nextIndex]);
          matchPointCounts();
        }
        
        // Draw morphing points
        ctx.fillStyle = '#3366ff';
        
        for (let i = 0; i < sourcePoints.length; i++) {
          const source = sourcePoints[i];
          const target = targetPoints[i];
          
          const x = source.x + (target.x - source.x) * progress;
          const y = source.y + (target.y - source.y) * progress;
          
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.arc(x, y, 1.5, 0, Math.PI * 2);
          ctx.fill();
        }
      } else {
        // Static display
        ctx.font = 'bold 80px Arial';
        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
        ctx.fillStyle = '#3366ff';
        ctx.fillText('MORPHING', width / 2, height / 2);
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // 3D particle sphere
  const render3DSphere = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    const centerX = width / 2;
    const centerY = height / 2;
    
    // Generate sphere points
    const points = [];
    const radius = 100;
    const resolution = 30;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < 800; i++) {
      // Random point on sphere using spherical coordinates
      const theta = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
      const phi = Math.acos(2 * Math.random() - 1);
      
      const x = radius * Math.sin(phi) * Math.cos(theta);
      const y = radius * Math.sin(phi) * Math.sin(theta);
      const z = radius * Math.cos(phi);
      
      points.push({ x, y, z, size: Math.random() * 2 + 1 });
    }
    
    let rotation = 0;
    let tiltX = 0;
    let tiltY = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update rotation
      if (isAnimating) {
        rotation += 0.005;
        tiltX = Math.sin(rotation * 0.5) * 0.3;
        tiltY = Math.cos(rotation * 0.5) * 0.2;
      }
      
      // Clear with gradient background
      const gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(centerX, centerY, 0, centerX, centerY, radius * 1.5);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(30, 30, 70, 1)');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(10, 10, 30, 1)');
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Sort points by z-index for correct drawing order
      const sortedPoints = [...points].sort((a, b) => {
        // Apply rotation transformations to z for sorting
        const cosRY = Math.cos(rotation);
        const sinRY = Math.sin(rotation);
        const cosRX = Math.cos(tiltX);
        const sinRX = Math.sin(tiltX);
        
        const aRotZ = a.z * cosRY - a.x * sinRY;
        const bRotZ = b.z * cosRY - b.x * sinRY;
        
        return aRotZ - bRotZ;
      });
      
      // Draw points
      sortedPoints.forEach(point => {
        // Apply rotation transformations
        const cosRY = Math.cos(rotation);
        const sinRY = Math.sin(rotation);
        const cosRX = Math.cos(tiltX);
        const sinRX = Math.sin(tiltX);
        
        // Rotate around Y axis
        const x1 = point.x * cosRY + point.z * sinRY;
        const z1 = point.z * cosRY - point.x * sinRY;
        
        // Rotate around X axis
        const y2 = point.y * cosRX + z1 * sinRX;
        const z2 = z1 * cosRX - point.y * sinRX;
        
        // Project 3D point to 2D screen
        const scale = 1000 / (1000 + z2);
        const projX = centerX + x1 * scale;
        const projY = centerY + y2 * scale;
        
        // Draw point with size and color based on depth
        const fillOpacity = 0.2 + 0.8 * ((z2 + radius) / (radius * 2));
        const glowOpacity = 0.1 + 0.3 * ((z2 + radius) / (radius * 2));
        const hue = (((z2 + radius) / (radius * 2)) * 120) + 180;
        
        // Glow effect
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(projX, projY, point.size * scale * 2, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${hue}, 100%, 70%, ${glowOpacity})`;
        ctx.fill();
        
        // Core of point
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(projX, projY, point.size * scale, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${hue}, 100%, 70%, ${fillOpacity})`;
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // DNA Helix
  const renderDNAHelix = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    const centerX = width / 2;
    
    let offset = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'black';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update animation
      if (isAnimating) {
        offset += 0.02;
      }
      
      const amplitude = 80;
      const frequency = 0.02;
      const step = 5;
      const strandSeparation = 20;
      
      // Draw helix
      for (let y = 0; y < height + step; y += step) {
        // Calculate sine wave positions
        const x1 = centerX + Math.sin((y * frequency) + offset) * amplitude;
        const x2 = centerX + Math.sin((y * frequency) + offset + Math.PI) * amplitude;
        
        // Draw main strands
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(x1, y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = '#ff3366';
        ctx.fill();
        
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(x2, y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = '#3366ff';
        ctx.fill();
        
        // Draw connecting lines at intervals
        if (y % 20 < step) {
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(x1, y);
          ctx.lineTo(x2, y);
          ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(200, 200, 200, 0.5)';
          ctx.lineWidth = 2;
          ctx.stroke();
        }
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Aurora effect
  const renderAurora = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Aurora waves
    const waves = [];
    const waveCount = 5;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < waveCount; i++) {
      waves.push({
        points: [],
        color: `hsla(${120 + i * 30}, 80%, 60%, 0.2)`,
        speed: 0.003 + i * 0.001,
        offset: i * 0.2
      });
      
      // Generate points for each wave
      const pointCount = Math.floor(width / 10);
      for (let j = 0; j < pointCount; j++) {
        waves[i].points.push({
          x: j * (width / (pointCount - 1)),
          y: 0,
          noiseOffset: Math.random() * 100
        });
      }
    }
    
    let time = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Background gradient
      const gradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, height);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, '#000510');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, '#001030');
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update animation time
      if (isAnimating) {
        time += 0.01;
      }
      
      // Draw stars
      for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
        const x = i * (width / 100) + Math.sin(time + i * 0.1) * 1;
        const y = (i % 20) * (height / 20) + Math.cos(time + i * 0.1) * 1;
        const size = Math.random() * 2 + 0.5;
        
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(x, y, size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8)';
        ctx.fill();
      }
      
      // Draw waves from back to front
      waves.forEach(wave => {
        // Update points
        wave.points.forEach(point => {
          const noiseValue = Math.sin(point.x * 0.02 + time * wave.speed + wave.offset);
          const waveHeight = height * 0.5;
          point.y = height * 0.7 + noiseValue * waveHeight;
        });
        
        // Draw wave
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(0, height);
        ctx.lineTo(wave.points[0].x, wave.points[0].y);
        
        for (let i = 1; i < wave.points.length; i++) {
          const xc = (wave.points[i].x + wave.points[i - 1].x) / 2;
          const yc = (wave.points[i].y + wave.points[i - 1].y) / 2;
          ctx.quadraticCurveTo(wave.points[i - 1].x, wave.points[i - 1].y, xc, yc);
        }
        
        ctx.lineTo(width, wave.points[wave.points.length - 1].y);
        ctx.lineTo(width, height);
        ctx.closePath();
        
        // Fill with gradient based on wave color
        const waveGradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, height);
        const baseColor = wave.color.substring(0, wave.color.lastIndexOf(',')) + ',';
        waveGradient.addColorStop(0, baseColor + ' 0.8)');
        waveGradient.addColorStop(1, baseColor + ' 0)');
        
        ctx.fillStyle = waveGradient;
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Initialize the current effect
  useEffect(() => {
    let effectInitializer;
    
    switch(activeEffect) {
      case 'galaxy':
        effectInitializer = renderGalaxy;
        break;
      case 'fire-text':
        effectInitializer = renderFireText;
        break;
      case 'particle-explosion':
        effectInitializer = renderParticleExplosion;
        break;
      case 'data-flow':
        effectInitializer = renderDataFlow;
        break;
      case 'glitch-text':
        effectInitializer = renderGlitchText;
        break;
      case 'morphing-text':
        effectInitializer = renderMorphingText;
        break;
      case '3d-sphere':
        effectInitializer = render3DSphere;
        break;
      case 'dna-helix':
        effectInitializer = renderDNAHelix;
        break;
      case 'aurora':
        effectInitializer = renderAurora;
        break;
    }
    
    if (effectInitializer) {
      effectInitializer();
    }
    
    return () => {
      if (animationRef.current) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);
      }
    };
  }, [activeEffect, isAnimating]);
  
  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 space-y-8">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Premium Particle & Text Effects</h1>
        
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-6">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('galaxy')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'galaxy' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Galaxy Simulation
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('fire-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'fire-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Fire Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('particle-explosion')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'particle-explosion' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Particle Explosion
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('data-flow')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'data-flow' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Data Flow Network
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('glitch-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'glitch-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Glitch Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('morphing-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'morphing-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Morphing Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('3d-sphere')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === '3d-sphere' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            3D Particle Sphere
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('dna-helix')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'dna-helix' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            DNA Helix
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('aurora')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'aurora' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Aurora Effect
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mb-4">
          <button 
            onClick={triggerAnimation} 
            className="px-6 py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors"
          >
            Preview Animation
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="border border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-100 min-h-64">
          <canvas 
            ref={canvasRef}
            width="800"
            height="400"
            className="w-full h-64 bg-black rounded"
          ></canvas>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Current Effect: {activeEffect}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-700">
            {activeEffect === 'galaxy' && 'A simulated galaxy with thousands of particles rotating around a central point with realistic physics and color gradients.'}
            {activeEffect === 'fire-text' && 'Text revealed through rising fire particles with realistic physics and color gradation from yellow to red.'}
            {activeEffect === 'particle-explosion' && 'Thousands of particles exploding outward with gravity and realistic motion, creating a spectacular burst effect.'}
            {activeEffect === 'data-flow' && 'Visualization of data flowing through a network with nodes and connections, perfect for tech interfaces.'}
            {activeEffect === 'glitch-text' && 'Text with advanced digital distortion effects including RGB shifting, scan lines, and noise for a cyberpunk aesthetic.'}
            {activeEffect === 'morphing-text' && 'Text that smoothly morphs between different words with individual points transforming in sequence.'}
            {activeEffect === '3d-sphere' && 'A 3D sphere of particles with realistic perspective, rotation, and depth-based coloring.'}
            {activeEffect === 'dna-helix' && 'A double-helix DNA animation with connecting strands and smooth rotation for scientific visualization.'}
            {activeEffect === 'aurora' && 'Simulated northern lights with flowing waves of color against a starry night sky background.'}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default PremiumParticleEffects;

import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';

const PremiumParticleEffects = () => {
  const [activeEffect, setActiveEffect] = useState('galaxy');
  const [isAnimating, setIsAnimating] = useState(false);
  const animationRef = useRef(null);
  const canvasRef = useRef(null);
  
  // Animation control
  const triggerAnimation = () => {
    setIsAnimating(true);
    setTimeout(() => setIsAnimating(false), 4000);
  };
  
  // Cancel animation when switching effects
  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      if (animationRef.current) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);
      }
    };
  }, [activeEffect]);
  
  // Galaxy particle system
  const renderGalaxy = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const centerX = canvas.width / 2;
    const centerY = canvas.height / 2;
    
    let particles = [];
    const particleCount = 2000;
    
    // Create particles
    for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
      const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
      const radius = Math.random() * 150;
      const spread = Math.random() * 0.3;
      const armOffset = (Math.random() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1) * spread;
      
      const x = centerX + Math.cos(angle + armOffset) * radius;
      const y = centerY + Math.sin(angle + armOffset) * radius;
      
      // Hue based on position in galaxy (creates spiral color pattern)
      const hue = (angle / (Math.PI * 2)) * 360;
      
      particles.push({
        x,
        y,
        radius: Math.random() * 2 + 0.5,
        angle,
        armOffset,
        distFromCenter: radius,
        hue,
        originalX: x,
        originalY: y,
        velocity: 0.01 + Math.random() * 0.01
      });
    }
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(10, 10, 20, 0.1)';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
      
      // Draw black hole at center
      const gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(centerX, centerY, 0, centerX, centerY, 30);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(30, 30, 80, 0.8)');
      gradient.addColorStop(0.5, 'rgba(20, 20, 50, 0.4)');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0, 0, 20, 0)');
      
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.arc(centerX, centerY, 30, 0, Math.PI * 2);
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fill();
      
      // Draw particles
      particles.forEach(particle => {
        if (isAnimating) {
          // Update particle position
          particle.angle += particle.velocity * (1 - particle.distFromCenter / 200);
          particle.x = centerX + Math.cos(particle.angle + particle.armOffset) * particle.distFromCenter;
          particle.y = centerY + Math.sin(particle.angle + particle.armOffset) * particle.distFromCenter;
        }
        
        // Draw particle
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(particle.x, particle.y, particle.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${particle.hue}, 80%, 70%, 0.8)`;
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Fire text effect
  const renderFireText = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Create text
    ctx.font = 'bold 40px Arial';
    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
    ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
    
    const text = 'FIRE TEXT';
    const textMeasure = ctx.measureText(text);
    const textWidth = textMeasure.width;
    
    // Create text mask
    ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
    const textData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
    
    // Fire particle system
    const particles = [];
    const particleCount = 2000;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
      const x = Math.random() * width;
      const y = height + Math.random() * 20;
      
      particles.push({
        x,
        y,
        radius: Math.random() * 2 + 1,
        color: `hsl(${Math.random() * 30 + 15}, 100%, ${Math.random() * 30 + 50}%)`,
        vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 2,
        vy: -Math.random() * 5 - 2
      });
    }
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Create a fade effect
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        particles.forEach(particle => {
          // Update particle position
          particle.x += particle.vx;
          particle.y += particle.vy;
          
          // Check if particle is inside text
          const pixelIndex = (Math.floor(particle.y) * width + Math.floor(particle.x)) * 4;
          const alpha = textData.data[pixelIndex + 3];
          
          if (alpha > 0) {
            particle.radius *= 0.9;
          }
          
          // Draw particle
          if (particle.radius > 0.1) {
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(particle.x, particle.y, particle.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.fillStyle = particle.color;
            ctx.fill();
          }
          
          // Reset particles that go off screen or get too small
          if (particle.y < 0 || particle.radius <= 0.1) {
            particle.x = Math.random() * width;
            particle.y = height + Math.random() * 20;
            particle.radius = Math.random() * 2 + 1;
            particle.color = `hsl(${Math.random() * 30 + 15}, 100%, ${Math.random() * 30 + 50}%)`;
          }
        });
      } else {
        // Draw static text when not animating
        ctx.font = 'bold 40px Arial';
        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
        ctx.fillStyle = '#ff6600';
        ctx.fillText('FIRE TEXT', width / 2, height / 2);
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Particle explosion
  const renderParticleExplosion = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    const centerX = width / 2;
    const centerY = height / 2;
    
    const particles = [];
    const particleCount = 1000;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
      const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
      const speed = Math.random() * 6 + 2;
      
      particles.push({
        x: centerX,
        y: centerY,
        radius: Math.random() * 3 + 1,
        color: `hsl(${Math.random() * 360}, 80%, 60%)`,
        vx: Math.cos(angle) * speed,
        vy: Math.sin(angle) * speed,
        life: 1,
        decay: Math.random() * 0.01 + 0.005
      });
    }
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        particles.forEach(particle => {
          // Update particle
          particle.x += particle.vx;
          particle.y += particle.vy;
          particle.vy += 0.1; // Gravity
          particle.life -= particle.decay;
          
          // Draw particle
          if (particle.life > 0) {
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(particle.x, particle.y, particle.radius * particle.life, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.fillStyle = particle.color;
            ctx.globalAlpha = particle.life;
            ctx.fill();
            ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
          }
        });
      } else {
        // Draw static text
        ctx.font = 'bold 30px Arial';
        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
        ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
        ctx.fillText('CLICK TO EXPLODE', centerX, centerY);
      }
      
      // Reset particles if all are dead
      if (isAnimating && particles.every(p => p.life <= 0)) {
        particles.forEach(particle => {
          const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
          const speed = Math.random() * 6 + 2;
          
          particle.x = centerX;
          particle.y = centerY;
          particle.vx = Math.cos(angle) * speed;
          particle.vy = Math.sin(angle) * speed;
          particle.life = 1;
        });
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Data flow particles
  const renderDataFlow = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Create digital circuit pattern
    const nodes = [];
    const connections = [];
    const nodeCount = 20;
    
    // Generate nodes (connection points)
    for (let i = 0; i < nodeCount; i++) {
      nodes.push({
        x: Math.random() * width,
        y: Math.random() * height,
        radius: Math.random() * 3 + 2
      });
    }
    
    // Generate connections between nodes
    for (let i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) {
      // Each node connects to 1-3 other nodes
      const connectionCount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
      
      for (let j = 0; j < connectionCount; j++) {
        // Find a random node to connect to
        const targetIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * nodes.length);
        if (targetIndex !== i) {
          connections.push({
            source: i,
            target: targetIndex,
            particles: [],
            pulseTime: Math.random() * 2000 + 1000
          });
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Generate particles for each connection
    connections.forEach(connection => {
      const particleCount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 5) + 3;
      for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
        connection.particles.push({
          position: Math.random(),
          speed: Math.random() * 0.01 + 0.003,
          size: Math.random() * 2 + 1
        });
      }
    });
    
    let lastTime = 0;
    
    const animate = (time) => {
      const deltaTime = time - lastTime;
      lastTime = time;
      
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Draw connections
      connections.forEach(connection => {
        const source = nodes[connection.source];
        const target = nodes[connection.target];
        
        // Draw connection line
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(source.x, source.y);
        ctx.lineTo(target.x, target.y);
        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(50, 130, 230, 0.2)';
        ctx.lineWidth = 1;
        ctx.stroke();
        
        // Calculate distance and angle
        const dx = target.x - source.x;
        const dy = target.y - source.y;
        const distance = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
        
        // Update and draw particles
        if (isAnimating) {
          connection.particles.forEach(particle => {
            // Update particle position
            particle.position += particle.speed;
            if (particle.position > 1) particle.position = 0;
            
            // Calculate position
            const x = source.x + dx * particle.position;
            const y = source.y + dy * particle.position;
            
            // Draw particle
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(x, y, particle.size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.fillStyle = '#00aaff';
            ctx.fill();
          });
        }
      });
      
      // Draw nodes
      nodes.forEach(node => {
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(node.x, node.y, node.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = '#005588';
        ctx.fill();
        
        // Glow effect
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(node.x, node.y, node.radius + 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 170, 255, 0.2)';
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate(0);
  };
  
  // Glitch text effect
  const renderGlitchText = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    const text = 'GLITCH';
    
    // Slice data for glitch effect
    const slices = [];
    const sliceCount = 20;
    const sliceHeight = height / sliceCount;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < sliceCount; i++) {
      slices.push({
        y: i * sliceHeight,
        offset: 0,
        glitchTime: 0,
        glitchDuration: 0
      });
    }
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'black';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Render text
      ctx.font = 'bold 60px "Courier New", monospace';
      ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        // Update glitch animation
        slices.forEach(slice => {
          slice.glitchTime--;
          
          if (slice.glitchTime <= 0) {
            // New glitch
            if (Math.random() < 0.1) {
              slice.glitchTime = Math.floor(Math.random() * 20) + 5;
              slice.glitchDuration = slice.glitchTime;
              slice.offset = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 40;
            }
          }
          
          // Draw slice
          ctx.save();
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.rect(0, slice.y, width, sliceHeight);
          ctx.clip();
          
          // RGB shift
          if (slice.glitchTime > 0) {
            const progress = slice.glitchTime / slice.glitchDuration;
            
            // Red channel
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgb(255, 0, 0)';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2 + slice.offset * progress, height / 2);
            
            // Green channel
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgb(0, 255, 0)';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
            
            // Blue channel
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgb(0, 0, 255)';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2 - slice.offset * progress, height / 2);
          } else {
            // Normal rendering
            ctx.fillStyle = 'white';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
          }
          
          ctx.restore();
        });
        
        // Random noise
        if (Math.random() < 0.1) {
          for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
            const noiseX = Math.random() * width;
            const noiseY = Math.random() * height;
            const noiseW = Math.random() * 40 + 10;
            const noiseH = Math.random() * 5 + 2;
            
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.5)';
            ctx.fillRect(noiseX, noiseY, noiseW, noiseH);
          }
        }
      } else {
        // Static display
        ctx.fillStyle = 'white';
        ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Morphing text effect
  const renderMorphingText = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Text to morph between
    const words = ['MORPH', 'TEXT', 'EFFECT'];
    let currentIndex = 0;
    let nextIndex = 1;
    let progress = 0;
    const morphSpeed = 0.01;
    
    // Generate points for text
    const generateTextPoints = (text) => {
      ctx.font = 'bold 80px Arial';
      ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
      
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
      
      const imageData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
      const pixels = imageData.data;
      const points = [];
      
      // Sample points
      const sampleSize = 3;
      for (let y = 0; y < height; y += sampleSize) {
        for (let x = 0; x < width; x += sampleSize) {
          const i = (y * width + x) * 4;
          if (pixels[i + 3] > 128) { // If pixel is opaque enough
            points.push({
              x,
              y,
              originX: x,
              originY: y
            });
          }
        }
      }
      
      return points;
    };
    
    let sourcePoints = generateTextPoints(words[currentIndex]);
    let targetPoints = generateTextPoints(words[nextIndex]);
    
    // Match point counts
    const matchPointCounts = () => {
      // Make source and target have the same number of points
      const minPoints = Math.min(sourcePoints.length, targetPoints.length);
      const maxPoints = Math.max(sourcePoints.length, targetPoints.length);
      
      if (sourcePoints.length < targetPoints.length) {
        // Add random existing points to source
        for (let i = minPoints; i < maxPoints; i++) {
          const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * minPoints);
          sourcePoints.push({ ...sourcePoints[randomIndex] });
        }
      } else if (targetPoints.length < sourcePoints.length) {
        // Add random existing points to target
        for (let i = minPoints; i < maxPoints; i++) {
          const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * minPoints);
          targetPoints.push({ ...targetPoints[randomIndex] });
        }
      }
    };
    
    matchPointCounts();
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        // Update progress
        progress += morphSpeed;
        
        if (progress >= 1) {
          progress = 0;
          currentIndex = nextIndex;
          nextIndex = (nextIndex + 1) % words.length;
          sourcePoints = targetPoints;
          targetPoints = generateTextPoints(words[nextIndex]);
          matchPointCounts();
        }
        
        // Draw morphing points
        ctx.fillStyle = '#3366ff';
        
        for (let i = 0; i < sourcePoints.length; i++) {
          const source = sourcePoints[i];
          const target = targetPoints[i];
          
          const x = source.x + (target.x - source.x) * progress;
          const y = source.y + (target.y - source.y) * progress;
          
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.arc(x, y, 1.5, 0, Math.PI * 2);
          ctx.fill();
        }
      } else {
        // Static display
        ctx.font = 'bold 80px Arial';
        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
        ctx.fillStyle = '#3366ff';
        ctx.fillText('MORPHING', width / 2, height / 2);
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // 3D particle sphere
  const render3DSphere = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    const centerX = width / 2;
    const centerY = height / 2;
    
    // Generate sphere points
    const points = [];
    const radius = 100;
    const resolution = 30;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < 800; i++) {
      // Random point on sphere using spherical coordinates
      const theta = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
      const phi = Math.acos(2 * Math.random() - 1);
      
      const x = radius * Math.sin(phi) * Math.cos(theta);
      const y = radius * Math.sin(phi) * Math.sin(theta);
      const z = radius * Math.cos(phi);
      
      points.push({ x, y, z, size: Math.random() * 2 + 1 });
    }
    
    let rotation = 0;
    let tiltX = 0;
    let tiltY = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update rotation
      if (isAnimating) {
        rotation += 0.005;
        tiltX = Math.sin(rotation * 0.5) * 0.3;
        tiltY = Math.cos(rotation * 0.5) * 0.2;
      }
      
      // Clear with gradient background
      const gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(centerX, centerY, 0, centerX, centerY, radius * 1.5);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(30, 30, 70, 1)');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(10, 10, 30, 1)');
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Sort points by z-index for correct drawing order
      const sortedPoints = [...points].sort((a, b) => {
        // Apply rotation transformations to z for sorting
        const cosRY = Math.cos(rotation);
        const sinRY = Math.sin(rotation);
        const cosRX = Math.cos(tiltX);
        const sinRX = Math.sin(tiltX);
        
        const aRotZ = a.z * cosRY - a.x * sinRY;
        const bRotZ = b.z * cosRY - b.x * sinRY;
        
        return aRotZ - bRotZ;
      });
      
      // Draw points
      sortedPoints.forEach(point => {
        // Apply rotation transformations
        const cosRY = Math.cos(rotation);
        const sinRY = Math.sin(rotation);
        const cosRX = Math.cos(tiltX);
        const sinRX = Math.sin(tiltX);
        
        // Rotate around Y axis
        const x1 = point.x * cosRY + point.z * sinRY;
        const z1 = point.z * cosRY - point.x * sinRY;
        
        // Rotate around X axis
        const y2 = point.y * cosRX + z1 * sinRX;
        const z2 = z1 * cosRX - point.y * sinRX;
        
        // Project 3D point to 2D screen
        const scale = 1000 / (1000 + z2);
        const projX = centerX + x1 * scale;
        const projY = centerY + y2 * scale;
        
        // Draw point with size and color based on depth
        const fillOpacity = 0.2 + 0.8 * ((z2 + radius) / (radius * 2));
        const glowOpacity = 0.1 + 0.3 * ((z2 + radius) / (radius * 2));
        const hue = (((z2 + radius) / (radius * 2)) * 120) + 180;
        
        // Glow effect
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(projX, projY, point.size * scale * 2, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${hue}, 100%, 70%, ${glowOpacity})`;
        ctx.fill();
        
        // Core of point
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(projX, projY, point.size * scale, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${hue}, 100%, 70%, ${fillOpacity})`;
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // DNA Helix
  const renderDNAHelix = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    const centerX = width / 2;
    
    let offset = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'black';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update animation
      if (isAnimating) {
        offset += 0.02;
      }
      
      const amplitude = 80;
      const frequency = 0.02;
      const step = 5;
      const strandSeparation = 20;
      
      // Draw helix
      for (let y = 0; y < height + step; y += step) {
        // Calculate sine wave positions
        const x1 = centerX + Math.sin((y * frequency) + offset) * amplitude;
        const x2 = centerX + Math.sin((y * frequency) + offset + Math.PI) * amplitude;
        
        // Draw main strands
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(x1, y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = '#ff3366';
        ctx.fill();
        
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(x2, y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = '#3366ff';
        ctx.fill();
        
        // Draw connecting lines at intervals
        if (y % 20 < step) {
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(x1, y);
          ctx.lineTo(x2, y);
          ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(200, 200, 200, 0.5)';
          ctx.lineWidth = 2;
          ctx.stroke();
        }
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Aurora effect
  const renderAurora = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Aurora waves
    const waves = [];
    const waveCount = 5;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < waveCount; i++) {
      waves.push({
        points: [],
        color: `hsla(${120 + i * 30}, 80%, 60%, 0.2)`,
        speed: 0.003 + i * 0.001,
        offset: i * 0.2
      });
      
      // Generate points for each wave
      const pointCount = Math.floor(width / 10);
      for (let j = 0; j < pointCount; j++) {
        waves[i].points.push({
          x: j * (width / (pointCount - 1)),
          y: 0,
          noiseOffset: Math.random() * 100
        });
      }
    }
    
    let time = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Background gradient
      const gradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, height);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, '#000510');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, '#001030');
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update animation time
      if (isAnimating) {
        time += 0.01;
      }
      
      // Draw stars
      for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
        const x = i * (width / 100) + Math.sin(time + i * 0.1) * 1;
        const y = (i % 20) * (height / 20) + Math.cos(time + i * 0.1) * 1;
        const size = Math.random() * 2 + 0.5;
        
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(x, y, size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8)';
        ctx.fill();
      }
      
      // Draw waves from back to front
      waves.forEach(wave => {
        // Update points
        wave.points.forEach(point => {
          const noiseValue = Math.sin(point.x * 0.02 + time * wave.speed + wave.offset);
          const waveHeight = height * 0.5;
          point.y = height * 0.7 + noiseValue * waveHeight;
        });
        
        // Draw wave
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(0, height);
        ctx.lineTo(wave.points[0].x, wave.points[0].y);
        
        for (let i = 1; i < wave.points.length; i++) {
          const xc = (wave.points[i].x + wave.points[i - 1].x) / 2;
          const yc = (wave.points[i].y + wave.points[i - 1].y) / 2;
          ctx.quadraticCurveTo(wave.points[i - 1].x, wave.points[i - 1].y, xc, yc);
        }
        
        ctx.lineTo(width, wave.points[wave.points.length - 1].y);
        ctx.lineTo(width, height);
        ctx.closePath();
        
        // Fill with gradient based on wave color
        const waveGradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, height);
        const baseColor = wave.color.substring(0, wave.color.lastIndexOf(',')) + ',';
        waveGradient.addColorStop(0, baseColor + ' 0.8)');
        waveGradient.addColorStop(1, baseColor + ' 0)');
        
        ctx.fillStyle = waveGradient;
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Initialize the current effect
  useEffect(() => {
    let effectInitializer;
    
    switch(activeEffect) {
      case 'galaxy':
        effectInitializer = renderGalaxy;
        break;
      case 'fire-text':
        effectInitializer = renderFireText;
        break;
      case 'particle-explosion':
        effectInitializer = renderParticleExplosion;
        break;
      case 'data-flow':
        effectInitializer = renderDataFlow;
        break;
      case 'glitch-text':
        effectInitializer = renderGlitchText;
        break;
      case 'morphing-text':
        effectInitializer = renderMorphingText;
        break;
      case '3d-sphere':
        effectInitializer = render3DSphere;
        break;
      case 'dna-helix':
        effectInitializer = renderDNAHelix;
        break;
      case 'aurora':
        effectInitializer = renderAurora;
        break;
    }
    
    if (effectInitializer) {
      effectInitializer();
    }
    
    return () => {
      if (animationRef.current) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);
      }
    };
  }, [activeEffect, isAnimating]);
  
  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 space-y-8">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Premium Particle & Text Effects</h1>
        
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-6">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('galaxy')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'galaxy' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Galaxy Simulation
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('fire-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'fire-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Fire Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('particle-explosion')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'particle-explosion' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Particle Explosion
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('data-flow')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'data-flow' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Data Flow Network
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('glitch-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'glitch-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Glitch Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('morphing-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'morphing-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Morphing Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('3d-sphere')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === '3d-sphere' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            3D Particle Sphere
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('dna-helix')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'dna-helix' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            DNA Helix
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('aurora')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'aurora' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Aurora Effect
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mb-4">
          <button 
            onClick={triggerAnimation} 
            className="px-6 py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors"
          >
            Preview Animation
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="border border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-100 min-h-64">
          <canvas 
            ref={canvasRef}
            width="800"
            height="400"
            className="w-full h-64 bg-black rounded"
          ></canvas>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Current Effect: {activeEffect}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-700">
            {activeEffect === 'galaxy' && 'A simulated galaxy with thousands of particles rotating around a central point with realistic physics and color gradients.'}
            {activeEffect === 'fire-text' && 'Text revealed through rising fire particles with realistic physics and color gradation from yellow to red.'}
            {activeEffect === 'particle-explosion' && 'Thousands of particles exploding outward with gravity and realistic motion, creating a spectacular burst effect.'}
            {activeEffect === 'data-flow' && 'Visualization of data flowing through a network with nodes and connections, perfect for tech interfaces.'}
            {activeEffect === 'glitch-text' && 'Text with advanced digital distortion effects including RGB shifting, scan lines, and noise for a cyberpunk aesthetic.'}
            {activeEffect === 'morphing-text' && 'Text that smoothly morphs between different words with individual points transforming in sequence.'}
            {activeEffect === '3d-sphere' && 'A 3D sphere of particles with realistic perspective, rotation, and depth-based coloring.'}
            {activeEffect === 'dna-helix' && 'A double-helix DNA animation with connecting strands and smooth rotation for scientific visualization.'}
            {activeEffect === 'aurora' && 'Simulated northern lights with flowing waves of color against a starry night sky background.'}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default PremiumParticleEffects;


import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

const AdvancedParticleEffects = () => {
  const [activeEffect, setActiveEffect] = useState('particle-swarm');
  const [isAnimating, setIsAnimating] = useState(false);
  const [animationFrame, setAnimationFrame] = useState(0);
  
  // Animation control
  const triggerAnimation = () => {
    setIsAnimating(true);
    setTimeout(() => setIsAnimating(false), 3000);
  };
  
  // Animation frame counter for continuous animations
  useEffect(() => {
    let frameId;
    if (isAnimating) {
      const animate = () => {
        setAnimationFrame(prev => prev + 1);
        frameId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
      };
      frameId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    }
    return () => {
      if (frameId) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(frameId);
      }
    };
  }, [isAnimating]);
  
  // Effect components
  const renderEffect = () => {
    switch(activeEffect) {
      case 'particle-swarm':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            {isAnimating && Array(50).fill().map((_, i) => {
              // Calculate particle properties
              const size = Math.random() * 8 + 2;
              const startX = Math.random() * 300 - 150;
              const startY = Math.random() * 300 - 150;
              const endX = Math.random() * 10 - 5;
              const endY = Math.random() * 10 - 5;
              const duration = Math.random() * 2 + 1;
              const delay = Math.random() * 0.5;
              const opacity = Math.random() * 0.6 + 0.4;
              
              return (
                <div 
                  key={i}
                  className="absolute rounded-full bg-blue-500"
                  style={{
                    width: `${size}px`,
                    height: `${size}px`,
                    left: 'calc(50% + 0px)',
                    top: 'calc(50% + 0px)',
                    opacity: opacity,
                    transform: `translate(${startX}px, ${startY}px)`,
                    transition: `transform ${duration}s ease-out ${delay}s`
                  }}
                >
                  <div 
                    className="w-full h-full rounded-full bg-blue-500 transition-transform"
                    style={{
                      transform: `translate(${endX}px, ${endY}px)`,
                      transition: `transform ${duration * 4}s ease-in-out`,
                      boxShadow: '0 0 4px rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.5)'
                    }}
                  />
                </div>
              );
            })}
            <div className="text-xl font-bold text-blue-600 z-10">Particle Swarm</div>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'fluid-simulation':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <svg width="100%" height="100%" viewBox="0 0 400 200">
              <defs>
                <linearGradient id="fluid-gradient" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
                  <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#2563eb" />
                  <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#7c3aed" />
                </linearGradient>
                <filter id="fluid-turbulence">
                  <feTurbulence 
                    type="fractalNoise" 
                    baseFrequency="0.01 0.01" 
                    seed="3" 
                    numOctaves="3" 
                    result="turbulence"
                    stitchTiles="stitch"
                  >
                    <animate 
                      attributeName="baseFrequency" 
                      values="0.01 0.01;0.02 0.02;0.01 0.01" 
                      dur="10s" 
                      repeatCount="indefinite"
                      begin={isAnimating ? "0s" : "indefinite"}
                    />
                  </feTurbulence>
                  <feDisplacementMap in="SourceGraphic" in2="turbulence" scale="30" xChannelSelector="R" yChannelSelector="G" />
                </filter>
              </defs>
              <g filter={isAnimating ? "url(#fluid-turbulence)" : ""}>
                <rect x="50" y="50" width="300" height="100" rx="20" fill="url(#fluid-gradient)" />
                <text x="200" y="105" textAnchor="middle" fill="white" fontSize="20" fontWeight="bold">
                  Fluid Distortion
                </text>
              </g>
            </svg>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'constellation':
        const numNodes = 12;
        const nodes = [];
        const connections = [];
        
        // Create nodes with fixed positions for consistency
        for (let i = 0; i < numNodes; i++) {
          const angle = (i / numNodes) * Math.PI * 2;
          const radius = Math.random() * 40 + 60;
          const x = Math.cos(angle) * radius + 150;
          const y = Math.sin(angle) * radius + 100;
          nodes.push({ id: i, x, y });
        }
        
        // Create connections between nodes
        for (let i = 0; i < numNodes; i++) {
          for (let j = i + 1; j < numNodes; j++) {
            const distance = Math.sqrt(
              Math.pow(nodes[i].x - nodes[j].x, 2) + 
              Math.pow(nodes[i].y - nodes[j].y, 2)
            );
            
            if (distance < 70) {
              connections.push({ 
                id: `${i}-${j}`, 
                source: i, 
                target: j, 
                distance 
              });
            }
          }
        }
        
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <svg width="100%" height="100%" viewBox="0 0 300 200">
              <g>
                {/* Draw connections */}
                {connections.map(conn => {
                  const source = nodes[conn.source];
                  const target = nodes[conn.target];
                  const opacity = isAnimating ? 
                    Math.max(0, 1 - (conn.distance / 100)) : 
                    Math.max(0, 0.5 - (conn.distance / 100));
                  
                  return (
                    <line 
                      key={conn.id}
                      x1={source.x} 
                      y1={source.y} 
                      x2={target.x} 
                      y2={target.y}
                      stroke="#4f46e5"
                      strokeWidth="1"
                      opacity={opacity}
                      className="transition-opacity duration-1000"
                    />
                  );
                })}
                
                {/* Draw nodes */}
                {nodes.map(node => (
                  <g key={node.id}>
                    <circle 
                      cx={node.x} 
                      cy={node.y} 
                      r={isAnimating ? 4 : 3}
                      fill={isAnimating ? "#3b82f6" : "#6366f1"}
                      className="transition-all duration-700"
                    />
                    {isAnimating && (
                      <circle 
                        cx={node.x} 
                        cy={node.y} 
                        r="8"
                        fill="none"
                        stroke="#93c5fd"
                        strokeWidth="1"
                        opacity="0.5"
                        className="animate-ping"
                      />
                    )}
                  </g>
                ))}
              </g>
            </svg>
            <div className="absolute bottom-4 text-center w-full text-indigo-600 font-semibold">
              Network Constellation
            </div>
          </div>
        );
                
      case 'particle-text':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <svg width="100%" height="100%" viewBox="0 0 300 100">
              <defs>
                <filter id="particle-disintegration" x="-20%" y="-20%" width="140%" height="140%">
                  <feTurbulence type="fractalNoise" baseFrequency="0.05" numOctaves="1" result="noise" />
                  <feDisplacementMap 
                    in="SourceGraphic" 
                    in2="noise" 
                    scale={isAnimating ? "20" : "0"} 
                    xChannelSelector="R" 
                    yChannelSelector="G" 
                  >
                    <animate 
                      attributeName="scale" 
                      values="0;20;0" 
                      dur="3s" 
                      begin={isAnimating ? "0s" : "indefinite"}
                    />
                  </feDisplacementMap>
                </filter>
              </defs>
              <text 
                x="150" 
                y="60" 
                textAnchor="middle" 
                filter="url(#particle-disintegration)"
                fill="#3b82f6"
                fontWeight="bold"
                fontSize="32"
              >
                DISINTEGRATE
              </text>
            </svg>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'energy-field':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <div className="w-64 h-48 rounded-lg bg-indigo-900 flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold relative overflow-hidden">
              <div className="z-10 relative">Energy Field</div>
              
              {/* Energy field particles */}
              {isAnimating && Array(20).fill().map((_, i) => {
                const delay = i * 0.1;
                const size = Math.random() * 10 + 5;
                const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
                const distance = Math.random() * 30 + 40;
                const duration = Math.random() * 2 + 1;
                const x = Math.cos(angle) * distance;
                const y = Math.sin(angle) * distance;
                
                return (
                  <div 
                    key={i}
                    className="absolute rounded-full bg-blue-400 opacity-70"
                    style={{
                      width: `${size}px`,
                      height: `${size}px`,
                      left: 'calc(50% - 4px)',
                      top: 'calc(50% - 4px)',
                      boxShadow: '0 0 15px rgba(96, 165, 250, 0.7)',
                      animation: `pulse ${duration}s ease-in-out infinite alternate`,
                      transform: `translate(${x}px, ${y}px) scale(${isAnimating ? 1 : 0})`,
                      transition: `transform ${duration}s ease-out ${delay}s`
                    }}
                  />
                );
              })}
              
              {/* Central glow */}
              <div 
                className="absolute w-24 h-24 rounded-full bg-blue-400 opacity-30 transition-all duration-1000"
                style={{
                  filter: 'blur(10px)',
                  transform: isAnimating ? 'scale(1.5)' : 'scale(0.8)',
                  animation: isAnimating ? 'pulse 2s ease-in-out infinite alternate' : 'none'
                }}
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'matrix-effect':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden bg-black">
            <div className="absolute inset-0 font-mono text-green-500 text-opacity-70 leading-none text-sm overflow-hidden">
              {isAnimating && Array(30).fill().map((_, i) => {
                const column = i % 15;
                const speed = Math.random() * 300 + 700;
                const chars = "01アイウエオカキクケコサシスセソタチツテトナニヌネノ";
                
                return (
                  <div 
                    key={i}
                    className="absolute"
                    style={{
                      left: `${column * 30 + 10}px`,
                      top: 0,
                      animation: `matrixDrop ${speed}ms linear infinite`,
                      animationDelay: `${i * 100}ms`
                    }}
                  >
                    {Array(20).fill().map((_, j) => {
                      const randomChar = chars[Math.floor(Math.random() * chars.length)];
                      return (
                        <div key={j} className="leading-none my-2">
                          {randomChar}
                        </div>
                      );
                    })}
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>
            <div className="text-green-400 text-2xl font-bold z-10 text-center">
              <div className={isAnimating ? "animate-pulse" : ""}>MATRIX RAIN</div>
            </div>
            <style jsx>{`
              @keyframes matrixDrop {
                0% { transform: translateY(-100%); }
                100% { transform: translateY(100%); }
              }
              @keyframes pulse {
                0% { opacity: 0.3; }
                100% { opacity: 0.7; }
              }
            `}</style>
          </div>
        );

      case 'water-ripple':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <div className="w-64 h-48 bg-gradient-to-b from-blue-300 to-blue-600 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center relative overflow-hidden">
              <div className="text-white text-xl font-bold z-10">Water Ripple</div>
              
              {isAnimating && Array(4).fill().map((_, i) => {
                const delay = i * 0.6;
                
                return (
                  <div 
                    key={i}
                    className="absolute rounded-full border border-white border-opacity-50 transition-all"
                    style={{
                      width: '20px',
                      height: '20px',
                      left: 'calc(50% - 10px)',
                      top: 'calc(50% - 10px)',
                      transform: `scale(${isAnimating ? 8 : 0})`,
                      opacity: isAnimating ? 0 : 1,
                      transition: `transform 3s ease-out ${delay}s, opacity 3s ease-out ${delay}s`
                    }}
                  />
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'electric-pulse':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <svg width="100%" height="100%" viewBox="0 0 300 200">
              <defs>
                <filter id="glow" x="-20%" y="-20%" width="140%" height="140%">
                  <feGaussianBlur stdDeviation="5" result="blur" />
                  <feComposite in="SourceGraphic" in2="blur" operator="over" />
                </filter>
              </defs>
              
              {/* Path for the electric arc */}
              <path 
                d={`M 50,100 
                   C 70,${isAnimating ? 70 : 100} 90,${isAnimating ? 130 : 100} 110,${isAnimating ? 90 : 100} 
                   C 130,${isAnimating ? 50 : 100} 150,${isAnimating ? 150 : 100} 170,${isAnimating ? 70 : 100}
                   C 190,${isAnimating ? 90 : 100} 210,${isAnimating ? 110 : 100} 250,${isAnimating ? 80 : 100}`}
                stroke="#60a5fa"
                strokeWidth="3"
                fill="none"
                filter="url(#glow)"
                className="transition-all duration-300"
                strokeDasharray={isAnimating ? "5,5" : "none"}
                opacity={isAnimating ? "0.8" : "0.3"}
              />
              
              {/* Nodes at either end */}
              <circle cx="50" cy="100" r="10" fill="#3b82f6" filter="url(#glow)" />
              <circle cx="250" cy="100" r="10" fill="#3b82f6" filter="url(#glow)" />
              
              {/* Pulsing glow when active */}
              {isAnimating && (
                <>
                  <circle cx="50" cy="100" r="15" fill="none" stroke="#93c5fd" strokeWidth="2" className="animate-ping" />
                  <circle cx="250" cy="100" r="15" fill="none" stroke="#93c5fd" strokeWidth="2" className="animate-ping" />
                </>
              )}
            </svg>
            <div className="absolute bottom-4 text-center w-full text-blue-600 font-semibold">
              Electric Pulse
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'confetti-explosion':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <button 
              className={`px-6 py-3 bg-purple-600 text-white rounded-lg shadow-lg transition-all ${isAnimating ? 'scale-105' : ''}`}
            >
              Celebrate!
            </button>
            
            {/* Confetti pieces */}
            {isAnimating && Array(80).fill().map((_, i) => {
              const colors = ['#ef4444', '#f59e0b', '#3b82f6', '#10b981', '#8b5cf6', '#ec4899'];
              const color = colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length)];
              const size = Math.random() * 8 + 4;
              const isSquare = Math.random() > 0.5;
              const angle = Math.random() * 360;
              const distance = Math.random() * 150 + 30;
              const startAngle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
              const x = Math.cos(startAngle) * distance;
              const y = Math.sin(startAngle) * distance;
              const rotateSpeed = Math.random() * 760 + 360;
              const delay = Math.random() * 0.5;
              
              return (
                <div 
                  key={i}
                  className="absolute transition-all"
                  style={{
                    width: `${size}px`,
                    height: isSquare ? `${size}px` : `${size * 0.4}px`,
                    borderRadius: isSquare ? '2px' : '0',
                    backgroundColor: color,
                    left: 'calc(50% - 4px)',
                    top: 'calc(50% - 4px)',
                    opacity: isAnimating ? 1 : 0,
                    transform: `translate(${x}px, ${y}px) rotate(${angle}deg)`,
                    transition: `transform 1s ease-out ${delay}s, opacity 0.8s ease-out ${delay}s`,
                    animation: `spin ${rotateSpeed}ms linear infinite`
                  }}
                />
              );
            })}
            
            <style jsx>{`
              @keyframes spin {
                from { transform: translate(${isAnimating ? 'var(--x, 0)' : '0'}px, ${isAnimating ? 'var(--y, 0)' : '0'}px) rotate(0deg); }
                to { transform: translate(${isAnimating ? 'var(--x, 0)' : '0'}px, ${isAnimating ? 'var(--y, 0)' : '0'}px) rotate(360deg); }
              }
            `}</style>
          </div>
        );
        
      default:
        return <div>Select an effect</div>;
    }
  };
  
  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 space-y-8">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Advanced Particle & Complex Animation Effects</h1>
        
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-6">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('particle-swarm')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'particle-swarm' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Particle Swarm
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('fluid-simulation')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'fluid-simulation' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Fluid Simulation
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('constellation')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'constellation' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Constellation
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('particle-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'particle-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Particle Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('energy-field')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'energy-field' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Energy Field
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('matrix-effect')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'matrix-effect' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Matrix Rain
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('water-ripple')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'water-ripple' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Water Ripple
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('electric-pulse')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'electric-pulse' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Electric Pulse
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('confetti-explosion')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'confetti-explosion' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Confetti Explosion
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mb-4">
          <button 
            onClick={triggerAnimation} 
            className="px-6 py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors"
          >
            Preview Animation
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="border border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-100 min-h-64">
          {renderEffect()}
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Current Effect: {activeEffect}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-700">
            {activeEffect === 'particle-swarm' && 'Dynamic particles that move and swarm around a central point with independent behaviors. Creates organic, lifelike motion.'}
            {activeEffect === 'fluid-simulation' && 'SVG-based fluid distortion effect that mimics liquid movement. Creates an organic, flowing distortion of content.'}
            {activeEffect === 'constellation' && 'Interactive network of connected nodes that responds to interaction. Perfect for data visualization or abstract backgrounds.'}
            {activeEffect === 'particle-text' && 'Text that disintegrates into particles using SVG turbulence filters. Creates dramatic transitions for text elements.'}
            {activeEffect === 'energy-field' && 'Glowing particles that orbit around a central point with pulsing energy. Great for sci-fi interfaces or power indicators.'}
            {activeEffect === 'matrix-effect' && 'Falling characters animation inspired by "The Matrix" films. Creates a distinctive digital rain effect.'}
