            if (bolt.segments.length > 2) {
              const segmentIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * (bolt.segments.length - 2)) + 1;
              createBranch(bolt, bolt.segments[segmentIndex]);
            }
          }
          
          bolts.push(bolt);
          lastStrikeTime = timestamp;
        }
        
        // Update bolts
        for (let i = bolts.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
          const bolt = bolts[i];
          bolt.age++;
          
          // Remove old bolts
          if (bolt.age >= bolt.maxAge) {
            bolts.splice(i, 1);
          }
        }
      }
      
      // Draw lightning bolts
      ctx.lineCap = 'round';
      ctx.lineJoin = 'round';
      
      bolts.forEach(bolt => {
        // Calculate opacity based on age
        const opacity = 1 - (bolt.age / bolt.maxAge);
        const width = 5 * opacity;
        
        // Draw main bolt with glow
        ctx.beginPath();
        
        if (bolt.segments.length > 0) {
          ctx.moveTo(bolt.segments[0].x, bolt.segments[0].y);
          
          for (let i = 1; i < bolt.segments.length; i++) {
            ctx.lineTo(bolt.segments[i].x, bolt.segments[i].y);
          }
        }
        
        // Outer glow
        ctx.strokeStyle = bolt.color.replace('70%)', '50%)');
        ctx.lineWidth = width * 3;
        ctx.globalAlpha = opacity * 0.3;
        ctx.stroke();
        
        // Inner glow
        ctx.strokeStyle = bolt.color;
        ctx.lineWidth = width;
        ctx.globalAlpha = opacity;
        ctx.stroke();
        
        // Core
        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.9)';
        ctx.lineWidth = width * 0.5;
        ctx.globalAlpha = opacity;
        ctx.stroke();
        
        ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
      });
      
      // Static lightning display when not animating
      if (!isAnimating && bolts.length === 0) {
        const staticBolt = createBolt();
        staticBolt.segments = generateLightningPath(staticBolt.startX, staticBolt.startY, staticBolt.endX, staticBolt.endY, 100);
        
        // Draw static bolt
        ctx.beginPath();
        
        if (staticBolt.segments.length > 0) {
          ctx.moveTo(staticBolt.segments[0].x, staticBolt.segments[0].y);
          
          for (let i = 1; i < staticBolt.segments.length; i++) {
            ctx.lineTo(staticBolt.segments[i].x, staticBolt.segments[i].y);
          }
        }
        
        // Outer glow
        ctx.strokeStyle = staticBolt.color.replace('70%)', '50%)');
        ctx.lineWidth = 12;
        ctx.globalAlpha = 0.3;
        ctx.stroke();
        
        // Inner glow
        ctx.strokeStyle = staticBolt.color;
        ctx.lineWidth = 5;
        ctx.globalAlpha = 0.8;
        ctx.stroke();
        
        // Core
        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.9)';
        ctx.lineWidth = 2;
        ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
        ctx.stroke();
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate(0);
  };
  
  // Fractal Tree
  const renderFractalTree = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Tree parameters
    const startX = width / 2;
    const startY = height - 50;
    const initialAngle = -Math.PI / 2; // Upward
    const initialLength = height / 4;
    
    // Wind parameters
    let windStrength = 0;
    let windAngle = 0;
    
    // Draw tree recursively
    const drawBranch = (x, y, length, angle, depth, maxDepth, hue, branchWidth) => {
      if (depth >= maxDepth) return;
      
      // Calculate end point
      const endX = x + Math.cos(angle) * length;
      const endY = y + Math.sin(angle) * length;
      
      // Draw branch
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(x, y);
      ctx.lineTo(endX, endY);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `hsl(${hue}, ${100 - depth * 10}%, ${30 + depth * 5}%)`;
      ctx.lineWidth = branchWidth;
      ctx.stroke();
      
      // Draw leaves at the ends of branches
      if (depth >= maxDepth - 1) {
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(endX, endY, branchWidth * 2, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = `hsl(${hue + 20}, 80%, 50%)`;
        ctx.fill();
        return;
      }
      
      // Recursively draw branches
      const leftAngle = angle - Math.PI / 8 - (Math.random() * 0.2);
      const rightAngle = angle + Math.PI / 8 + (Math.random() * 0.2);
      
      drawBranch(endX, endY, length * 0.78, leftAngle, depth + 1, maxDepth, hue - 5, branchWidth * 0.8);
      drawBranch(endX, endY, length * 0.78, rightAngle, depth + 1, maxDepth, hue + 5, branchWidth * 0.8);
    };
    
    let time = 0;
    const growthDuration = 5000; // 5 seconds to fully grow
    let treeDepth = 0;
    
    const animate = (timestamp) => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update time and wind
      if (isAnimating) {
        time += 16; // Approximate milliseconds per frame
        treeDepth = Math.min(10, Math.floor((time / growthDuration) * 10));
        
        // Update wind
        windStrength = Math.sin(time / 1000) * 0.1;
        windAngle = initialAngle + windStrength;
      } else {
        treeDepth = 10; // Fully grown when static
      }
      
      // Draw ground
      const groundGradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, height - 60, 0, height);
      groundGradient.addColorStop(0, '#3a5a40');
      groundGradient.addColorStop(1, '#2b2d42');
      
      ctx.fillStyle = groundGradient;
      ctx.fillRect(0, height - 60, width, 60);
      
      // Draw tree
      drawBranch(startX, startY, initialLength, windAngle, 0, treeDepth, 120, 12);
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate(0);
  };
  
  // Caustics (light refraction)
  const renderCaustics = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Caustics parameters
    const causticLayers = 3;
    const causticPoints = 50;
    
    // Create caustic meshes
    const caustics = [];
    
    for (let layer = 0; layer < causticLayers; layer++) {
      const points = [];
      const controlPoints = [];
      
      // Create control points
      for (let i = 0; i <= causticPoints; i++) {
        controlPoints.push([]);
        
        for (let j = 0; j <= causticPoints; j++) {
          controlPoints[i].push({
            x: (width / causticPoints) * j,
            y: (height / causticPoints) * i,
            origX: (width / causticPoints) * j,
            origY: (height / causticPoints) * i
          });
        }
      }
      
      caustics.push({
        controlPoints,
        color: `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${0.1 + layer * 0.1})`,
        speed: 0.001 + layer * 0.001
      });
    }
    
    let time = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Draw underwater background
      const gradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, height);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, '#0077b6');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, '#03045e');
      
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        time += 0.01;
      }
      
      // Update and draw caustics
      caustics.forEach((caustic, layerIndex) => {
        // Update control points based on wave motion
        for (let i = 0; i <= causticPoints; i++) {
          for (let j = 0; j <= causticPoints; j++) {
            const point = caustic.controlPoints[i][j];
            
            // Apply wave distortion
            if (isAnimating) {
              const distortionX = Math.sin((i / causticPoints * 6) + time * caustic.speed * 10) * 10;
              const distortionY = Math.cos((j / causticPoints * 6) + time * caustic.speed * 10) * 10;
              
              point.x = point.origX + distortionX;
              point.y = point.origY + distortionY;
            } else {
              point.x = point.origX;
              point.y = point.origY;
            }
          }
        }
        
        // Draw mesh
        for (let i = 0; i < causticPoints; i++) {
          for (let j = 0; j < causticPoints; j++) {
            const p1 = caustic.controlPoints[i][j];
            const p2 = caustic.controlPoints[i + 1][j];
            const p3 = caustic.controlPoints[i + 1][j + 1];
            const p4 = caustic.controlPoints[i][j + 1];
            
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.moveTo(p1.x, p1.y);
            ctx.lineTo(p2.x, p2.y);
            ctx.lineTo(p3.x, p3.y);
            ctx.lineTo(p4.x, p4.y);
            ctx.closePath();
            
            // Calculate intensity based on distortion
            const avgX = (p1.x + p2.x + p3.x + p4.x) / 4;
            const avgY = (p1.y + p2.y + p3.y + p4.y) / 4;
            const origAvgX = (p1.origX + p2.origX + p3.origX + p4.origX) / 4;
            const origAvgY = (p1.origY + p2.origY + p3.origY + p4.origY) / 4;
            
            const distortion = Math.sqrt(
              Math.pow(avgX - origAvgX, 2) + 
              Math.pow(avgY - origAvgY, 2)
            );
            
            // Higher distortion = higher intensity
            const intensity = Math.min(1, distortion / 10);
            
            ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${intensity * 0.2})`;
            ctx.fill();
          }
        }
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Lava lamp effect
  const renderLavaLamp = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Lava blobs
    const blobs = [];
    const blobCount = 12;
    
    // Blob parameters
    const minRadius = 20;
    const maxRadius = 50;
    
    // Create blobs
    for (let i = 0; i < blobCount; i++) {
      blobs.push({
        x: Math.random() * width,
        y: Math.random() * height,
        radius: Math.random() * (maxRadius - minRadius) + minRadius,
        vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5,
        vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5,
        hue: Math.random() * 30 + 350, // Red to purple hues
        targetRadius: Math.random() * (maxRadius - minRadius) + minRadius,
        radiusVelocity: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2,
        phase: Math.random() * Math.PI * 2 // For oscillation
      });
    }
    
    let time = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      // Semi-transparent clear for trail effect
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Create background gradient
      const gradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, height);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, '#3a0061');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, '#121063');
      
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        time += 0.01;
      }
      
      // Update and draw blobs
      ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';
      
      // First pass: draw blobs
      blobs.forEach(blob => {
        if (isAnimating) {
          // Update position with random motion
          blob.x += blob.vx + Math.sin(time * 0.5 + blob.phase) * 0.2;
          blob.y += blob.vy - 0.1 + Math.cos(time * 0.5 + blob.phase) * 0.2; // Slight upward bias
          
          // Update radius
          blob.radius += blob.radiusVelocity;
          
          // Reverse direction if radius gets too small or too large
          if (blob.radius < minRadius || blob.radius > maxRadius) {
            blob.radiusVelocity *= -1;
          }
          
          // Bounce off edges with momentum transfer
          if (blob.x - blob.radius < 0) {
            blob.x = blob.radius;
            blob.vx *= -0.8;
          }
          if (blob.x + blob.radius > width) {
            blob.x = width - blob.radius;
            blob.vx *= -0.8;
          }
          if (blob.y - blob.radius < 0) {
            blob.y = blob.radius;
            blob.vy *= -0.8;
          }
          if (blob.y + blob.radius > height) {
            blob.y = height - blob.radius;
            blob.vy *= -0.8;
          }
          
          // Apply gradual velocity changes
          blob.vx += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.01;
          blob.vy += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.01;
          
          // Limit velocity
          const maxVel = 0.5;
          blob.vx = Math.max(-maxVel, Math.min(maxVel, blob.vx));
          blob.vy = Math.max(-maxVel, Math.min(maxVel, blob.vy));
        }
        
        // Draw blob as gradient
        const gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(
          blob.x, blob.y, 0,
          blob.x, blob.y, blob.radius
        );
        
        gradient.addColorStop(0, `hsla(${blob.hue}, 100%, 70%, 0.7)`);
        gradient.addColorStop(0.8, `hsla(${blob.hue}, 100%, 50%, 0.5)`);
        gradient.addColorStop(1, `hsla(${blob.hue}, 100%, 50%, 0)`);
        
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(blob.x, blob.y, blob.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      // Second pass: draw blob interactions (where blobs overlap)
      ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
      
      // Reset composite operation
      ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
      
      // Draw lamp container
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.rect(0, 0, width, height);
      ctx.lineWidth = 10;
      ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(20, 20, 20, 0.5)';
      ctx.stroke();
      
      // Draw lamp base
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.rect(width / 2 - 50, height - 20, 100, 20);
      ctx.fillStyle = '#222';
      ctx.fill();
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Initialize the current effect
  useEffect(() => {
    let effectInitializer;
    
    switch(activeEffect) {
      case 'flocking':
        effectInitializer = renderFlocking;
        break;
      case 'metaballs':
        effectInitializer = renderMetaballs;
        break;
      case 'ink-water':
        effectInitializer = renderInkInWater;
        break;
      case 'game-of-life':
        effectInitializer = renderGameOfLife;
        break;
      case 'cloth':
        effectInitializer = renderClothSimulation;
        break;
      case 'magnetic':
        effectInitializer = renderMagneticField;
        break;
      case 'lightning':
        effectInitializer = renderLightning;
        break;
      case 'fractal-tree':
        effectInitializer = renderFractalTree;
        break;
      case 'caustics':
        effectInitializer = renderCaustics;
        break;
      case 'lava-lamp':
        effectInitializer = renderLavaLamp;
        break;
    }
    
    if (effectInitializer) {
      effectInitializer();
    }
    
    return () => {
      if (animationRef.current) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);
      }
    };
  }, [activeEffect, isAnimating]);
  
  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 space-y-8">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Advanced Physics & Simulation Effects</h1>
        
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-6">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('flocking')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'flocking' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Flocking (Boids)
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('metaballs')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'metaballs' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Metaballs
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('ink-water')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'ink-water' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Ink in Water
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('game-of-life')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'game-of-life' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Game of Life
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('cloth')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'cloth' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Cloth Physics
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('magnetic')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'magnetic' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Magnetic Field
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('lightning')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'lightning' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Lightning
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('fractal-tree')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'fractal-tree' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Fractal Tree
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('caustics')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'caustics' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Caustics
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('lava-lamp')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'lava-lamp' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Lava Lamp
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mb-4">
          <button 
            onClick={triggerAnimation} 
            className="px-6 py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors"
          >
            Preview Animation
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="border border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-100 min-h-64">
          <canvas 
            ref={canvasRef}
            width="800"
            height="400"
            className="w-full h-64 bg-black rounded"
          ></canvas>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Current Effect: {activeEffect}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-700">
            {activeEffect === 'flocking' && 'Flocking behavior simulation (Boids algorithm) that mimics how birds or fish move in groups. Each entity follows three simple rules: separation, alignment, and cohesion, creating emergent complex behavior.'}
            {activeEffect === 'metaballs' && 'Metaballs (marching blob) effect that simulates the behavior of liquid mercury or lava lamp blobs. The blobs merge and separate organically when they come close to each other.'}
            {activeEffect === 'ink-water' && 'Simulation of ink or dye diffusing in water with realistic turbulence and flow. Shows how pigment spreads through liquid with natural physics.'}
            {activeEffect === 'game-of-life' && 'Conway\'s Game of Life cellular automaton where each cell follows simple rules that create complex emergent patterns. Demonstrates how simple rules can create complex systems.'}
            {activeEffect === 'cloth' && 'Physics-based cloth simulation using a network of connected points with constraints. Shows how fabric moves, folds, and responds to forces like wind and gravity.'}
            {activeEffect === 'magnetic' && 'Visualization of magnetic field lines between positive and negative poles. Shows how invisible fields can be represented visually with flow lines.'}
            {activeEffect === 'lightning' && 'Procedural lightning generation with realistic branching patterns. Creates natural-looking electrical discharges with fractal-like behavior.'}
            {activeEffect === 'fractal-tree' && 'Recursively generated tree that grows naturally with branches splitting at various angles. Demonstrates the beauty of fractal geometry in plant structures.'}
            {activeEffect === 'caustics' && 'Simulation of light patterns created by water refraction, like the dancing patterns on a pool floor. Creates organic, rippling light effects.'}
            {activeEffect === 'lava-lamp' && 'Physics simulation of blobs rising and falling with heat convection, merging and separating like in a real lava lamp. Shows fluid dynamics with colorful visuals.'}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default AdvancedSimulationEffects;


import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';

const PremiumParticleEffects = () => {
  const [activeEffect, setActiveEffect] = useState('galaxy');
  const [isAnimating, setIsAnimating] = useState(false);
  const animationRef = useRef(null);
  const canvasRef = useRef(null);
  
  // Animation control
  const triggerAnimation = () => {
    setIsAnimating(true);
    setTimeout(() => setIsAnimating(false), 4000);
  };
  
  // Cancel animation when switching effects
  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      if (animationRef.current) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);
      }
    };
  }, [activeEffect]);
  
  // Galaxy particle system
  const renderGalaxy = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const centerX = canvas.width / 2;
    const centerY = canvas.height / 2;
    
    let particles = [];
    const particleCount = 2000;
    
    // Create particles
    for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
      const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
      const radius = Math.random() * 150;
      const spread = Math.random() * 0.3;
      const armOffset = (Math.random() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1) * spread;
      
      const x = centerX + Math.cos(angle + armOffset) * radius;
      const y = centerY + Math.sin(angle + armOffset) * radius;
      
      // Hue based on position in galaxy (creates spiral color pattern)
      const hue = (angle / (Math.PI * 2)) * 360;
      
      particles.push({
        x,
        y,
        radius: Math.random() * 2 + 0.5,
        angle,
        armOffset,
        distFromCenter: radius,
        hue,
        originalX: x,
        originalY: y,
        velocity: 0.01 + Math.random() * 0.01
      });
    }
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(10, 10, 20, 0.1)';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
      
      // Draw black hole at center
      const gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(centerX, centerY, 0, centerX, centerY, 30);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(30, 30, 80, 0.8)');
      gradient.addColorStop(0.5, 'rgba(20, 20, 50, 0.4)');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0, 0, 20, 0)');
      
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.arc(centerX, centerY, 30, 0, Math.PI * 2);
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fill();
      
      // Draw particles
      particles.forEach(particle => {
        if (isAnimating) {
          // Update particle position
          particle.angle += particle.velocity * (1 - particle.distFromCenter / 200);
          particle.x = centerX + Math.cos(particle.angle + particle.armOffset) * particle.distFromCenter;
          particle.y = centerY + Math.sin(particle.angle + particle.armOffset) * particle.distFromCenter;
        }
        
        // Draw particle
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(particle.x, particle.y, particle.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${particle.hue}, 80%, 70%, 0.8)`;
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Fire text effect
  const renderFireText = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Create text
    ctx.font = 'bold 40px Arial';
    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
    ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
    
    const text = 'FIRE TEXT';
    const textMeasure = ctx.measureText(text);
    const textWidth = textMeasure.width;
    
    // Create text mask
    ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
    const textData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
    
    // Fire particle system
    const particles = [];
    const particleCount = 2000;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
      const x = Math.random() * width;
      const y = height + Math.random() * 20;
      
      particles.push({
        x,
        y,
        radius: Math.random() * 2 + 1,
        color: `hsl(${Math.random() * 30 + 15}, 100%, ${Math.random() * 30 + 50}%)`,
        vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 2,
        vy: -Math.random() * 5 - 2
      });
    }
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Create a fade effect
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        particles.forEach(particle => {
          // Update particle position
          particle.x += particle.vx;
          particle.y += particle.vy;
          
          // Check if particle is inside text
          const pixelIndex = (Math.floor(particle.y) * width + Math.floor(particle.x)) * 4;
          const alpha = textData.data[pixelIndex + 3];
          
          if (alpha > 0) {
            particle.radius *= 0.9;
          }
          
          // Draw particle
          if (particle.radius > 0.1) {
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(particle.x, particle.y, particle.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.fillStyle = particle.color;
            ctx.fill();
          }
          
          // Reset particles that go off screen or get too small
          if (particle.y < 0 || particle.radius <= 0.1) {
            particle.x = Math.random() * width;
            particle.y = height + Math.random() * 20;
            particle.radius = Math.random() * 2 + 1;
            particle.color = `hsl(${Math.random() * 30 + 15}, 100%, ${Math.random() * 30 + 50}%)`;
          }
        });
      } else {
        // Draw static text when not animating
        ctx.font = 'bold 40px Arial';
        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
        ctx.fillStyle = '#ff6600';
        ctx.fillText('FIRE TEXT', width / 2, height / 2);
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Particle explosion
  const renderParticleExplosion = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    const centerX = width / 2;
    const centerY = height / 2;
    
    const particles = [];
    const particleCount = 1000;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
      const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
      const speed = Math.random() * 6 + 2;
      
      particles.push({
        x: centerX,
        y: centerY,
        radius: Math.random() * 3 + 1,
        color: `hsl(${Math.random() * 360}, 80%, 60%)`,
        vx: Math.cos(angle) * speed,
        vy: Math.sin(angle) * speed,
        life: 1,
        decay: Math.random() * 0.01 + 0.005
      });
    }
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        particles.forEach(particle => {
          // Update particle
          particle.x += particle.vx;
          particle.y += particle.vy;
          particle.vy += 0.1; // Gravity
          particle.life -= particle.decay;
          
          // Draw particle
          if (particle.life > 0) {
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(particle.x, particle.y, particle.radius * particle.life, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.fillStyle = particle.color;
            ctx.globalAlpha = particle.life;
            ctx.fill();
            ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
          }
        });
      } else {
        // Draw static text
        ctx.font = 'bold 30px Arial';
        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
        ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
        ctx.fillText('CLICK TO EXPLODE', centerX, centerY);
      }
      
      // Reset particles if all are dead
      if (isAnimating && particles.every(p => p.life <= 0)) {
        particles.forEach(particle => {
          const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
          const speed = Math.random() * 6 + 2;
          
          particle.x = centerX;
          particle.y = centerY;
          particle.vx = Math.cos(angle) * speed;
          particle.vy = Math.sin(angle) * speed;
          particle.life = 1;
        });
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Data flow particles
  const renderDataFlow = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Create digital circuit pattern
    const nodes = [];
    const connections = [];
    const nodeCount = 20;
    
    // Generate nodes (connection points)
    for (let i = 0; i < nodeCount; i++) {
      nodes.push({
        x: Math.random() * width,
        y: Math.random() * height,
        radius: Math.random() * 3 + 2
      });
    }
    
    // Generate connections between nodes
    for (let i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) {
      // Each node connects to 1-3 other nodes
      const connectionCount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
      
      for (let j = 0; j < connectionCount; j++) {
        // Find a random node to connect to
        const targetIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * nodes.length);
        if (targetIndex !== i) {
          connections.push({
            source: i,
            target: targetIndex,
            particles: [],
            pulseTime: Math.random() * 2000 + 1000
          });
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Generate particles for each connection
    connections.forEach(connection => {
      const particleCount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 5) + 3;
      for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
        connection.particles.push({
          position: Math.random(),
          speed: Math.random() * 0.01 + 0.003,
          size: Math.random() * 2 + 1
        });
      }
    });
    
    let lastTime = 0;
    
    const animate = (time) => {
      const deltaTime = time - lastTime;
      lastTime = time;
      
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Draw connections
      connections.forEach(connection => {
        const source = nodes[connection.source];
        const target = nodes[connection.target];
        
        // Draw connection line
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(source.x, source.y);
        ctx.lineTo(target.x, target.y);
        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(50, 130, 230, 0.2)';
        ctx.lineWidth = 1;
        ctx.stroke();
        
        // Calculate distance and angle
        const dx = target.x - source.x;
        const dy = target.y - source.y;
        const distance = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
        
        // Update and draw particles
        if (isAnimating) {
          connection.particles.forEach(particle => {
            // Update particle position
            particle.position += particle.speed;
            if (particle.position > 1) particle.position = 0;
            
            // Calculate position
            const x = source.x + dx * particle.position;
            const y = source.y + dy * particle.position;
            
            // Draw particle
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(x, y, particle.size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.fillStyle = '#00aaff';
            ctx.fill();
          });
        }
      });
      
      // Draw nodes
      nodes.forEach(node => {
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(node.x, node.y, node.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = '#005588';
        ctx.fill();
        
        // Glow effect
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(node.x, node.y, node.radius + 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 170, 255, 0.2)';
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate(0);
  };
  
  // Glitch text effect
  const renderGlitchText = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    const text = 'GLITCH';
    
    // Slice data for glitch effect
    const slices = [];
    const sliceCount = 20;
    const sliceHeight = height / sliceCount;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < sliceCount; i++) {
      slices.push({
        y: i * sliceHeight,
        offset: 0,
        glitchTime: 0,
        glitchDuration: 0
      });
    }
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'black';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Render text
      ctx.font = 'bold 60px "Courier New", monospace';
      ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        // Update glitch animation
        slices.forEach(slice => {
          slice.glitchTime--;
          
          if (slice.glitchTime <= 0) {
            // New glitch
            if (Math.random() < 0.1) {
              slice.glitchTime = Math.floor(Math.random() * 20) + 5;
              slice.glitchDuration = slice.glitchTime;
              slice.offset = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 40;
            }
          }
          
          // Draw slice
          ctx.save();
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.rect(0, slice.y, width, sliceHeight);
          ctx.clip();
          
          // RGB shift
          if (slice.glitchTime > 0) {
            const progress = slice.glitchTime / slice.glitchDuration;
            
            // Red channel
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgb(255, 0, 0)';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2 + slice.offset * progress, height / 2);
            
            // Green channel
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgb(0, 255, 0)';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
            
            // Blue channel
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgb(0, 0, 255)';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2 - slice.offset * progress, height / 2);
          } else {
            // Normal rendering
            ctx.fillStyle = 'white';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
          }
          
          ctx.restore();
        });
        
        // Random noise
        if (Math.random() < 0.1) {
          for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
            const noiseX = Math.random() * width;
            const noiseY = Math.random() * height;
            const noiseW = Math.random() * 40 + 10;
            const noiseH = Math.random() * 5 + 2;
            
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.5)';
            ctx.fillRect(noiseX, noiseY, noiseW, noiseH);
          }
        }
      } else {
        // Static display
        ctx.fillStyle = 'white';
        ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Morphing text effect
  const renderMorphingText = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Text to morph between
    const words = ['MORPH', 'TEXT', 'EFFECT'];
    let currentIndex = 0;
    let nextIndex = 1;
    let progress = 0;
    const morphSpeed = 0.01;
    
    // Generate points for text
    const generateTextPoints = (text) => {
      ctx.font = 'bold 80px Arial';
      ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
      
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
      
      const imageData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
      const pixels = imageData.data;
      const points = [];
      
      // Sample points
      const sampleSize = 3;
      for (let y = 0; y < height; y += sampleSize) {
        for (let x = 0; x < width; x += sampleSize) {
          const i = (y * width + x) * 4;
          if (pixels[i + 3] > 128) { // If pixel is opaque enough
            points.push({
              x,
              y,
              originX: x,
              originY: y
            });
          }
        }
      }
      
      return points;
    };
    
    let sourcePoints = generateTextPoints(words[currentIndex]);
    let targetPoints = generateTextPoints(words[nextIndex]);
    
    // Match point counts
    const matchPointCounts = () => {
      // Make source and target have the same number of points
      const minPoints = Math.min(sourcePoints.length, targetPoints.length);
      const maxPoints = Math.max(sourcePoints.length, targetPoints.length);
      
      if (sourcePoints.length < targetPoints.length) {
        // Add random existing points to source
        for (let i = minPoints; i < maxPoints; i++) {
          const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * minPoints);
          sourcePoints.push({ ...sourcePoints[randomIndex] });
        }
      } else if (targetPoints.length < sourcePoints.length) {
        // Add random existing points to target
        for (let i = minPoints; i < maxPoints; i++) {
          const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * minPoints);
          targetPoints.push({ ...targetPoints[randomIndex] });
        }
      }
    };
    
    matchPointCounts();
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        // Update progress
        progress += morphSpeed;
        
        if (progress >= 1) {
          progress = 0;
          currentIndex = nextIndex;
          nextIndex = (nextIndex + 1) % words.length;
          sourcePoints = targetPoints;
          targetPoints = generateTextPoints(words[nextIndex]);
          matchPointCounts();
        }
        
        // Draw morphing points
        ctx.fillStyle = '#3366ff';
        
        for (let i = 0; i < sourcePoints.length; i++) {
          const source = sourcePoints[i];
          const target = targetPoints[i];
          
          const x = source.x + (target.x - source.x) * progress;
          const y = source.y + (target.y - source.y) * progress;
          
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.arc(x, y, 1.5, 0, Math.PI * 2);
          ctx.fill();
        }
      } else {
        // Static display
        ctx.font = 'bold 80px Arial';
        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
        ctx.fillStyle = '#3366ff';
        ctx.fillText('MORPHING', width / 2, height / 2);
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // 3D particle sphere
  const render3DSphere = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    const centerX = width / 2;
    const centerY = height / 2;
    
    // Generate sphere points
    const points = [];
    const radius = 100;
    const resolution = 30;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < 800; i++) {
      // Random point on sphere using spherical coordinates
      const theta = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
      const phi = Math.acos(2 * Math.random() - 1);
      
      const x = radius * Math.sin(phi) * Math.cos(theta);
      const y = radius * Math.sin(phi) * Math.sin(theta);
      const z = radius * Math.cos(phi);
      
      points.push({ x, y, z, size: Math.random() * 2 + 1 });
    }
    
    let rotation = 0;
    let tiltX = 0;
    let tiltY = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update rotation
      if (isAnimating) {
        rotation += 0.005;
        tiltX = Math.sin(rotation * 0.5) * 0.3;
        tiltY = Math.cos(rotation * 0.5) * 0.2;
      }
      
      // Clear with gradient background
      const gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(centerX, centerY, 0, centerX, centerY, radius * 1.5);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(30, 30, 70, 1)');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(10, 10, 30, 1)');
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Sort points by z-index for correct drawing order
      const sortedPoints = [...points].sort((a, b) => {
        // Apply rotation transformations to z for sorting
        const cosRY = Math.cos(rotation);
        const sinRY = Math.sin(rotation);
        const cosRX = Math.cos(tiltX);
        const sinRX = Math.sin(tiltX);
        
        const aRotZ = a.z * cosRY - a.x * sinRY;
        const bRotZ = b.z * cosRY - b.x * sinRY;
        
        return aRotZ - bRotZ;
      });
      
      // Draw points
      sortedPoints.forEach(point => {
        // Apply rotation transformations
        const cosRY = Math.cos(rotation);
        const sinRY = Math.sin(rotation);
        const cosRX = Math.cos(tiltX);
        const sinRX = Math.sin(tiltX);
        
        // Rotate around Y axis
        const x1 = point.x * cosRY + point.z * sinRY;
        const z1 = point.z * cosRY - point.x * sinRY;
        
        // Rotate around X axis
        const y2 = point.y * cosRX + z1 * sinRX;
        const z2 = z1 * cosRX - point.y * sinRX;
        
        // Project 3D point to 2D screen
        const scale = 1000 / (1000 + z2);
        const projX = centerX + x1 * scale;
        const projY = centerY + y2 * scale;
        
        // Draw point with size and color based on depth
        const fillOpacity = 0.2 + 0.8 * ((z2 + radius) / (radius * 2));
        const glowOpacity = 0.1 + 0.3 * ((z2 + radius) / (radius * 2));
        const hue = (((z2 + radius) / (radius * 2)) * 120) + 180;
        
        // Glow effect
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(projX, projY, point.size * scale * 2, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${hue}, 100%, 70%, ${glowOpacity})`;
        ctx.fill();
        
        // Core of point
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(projX, projY, point.size * scale, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${hue}, 100%, 70%, ${fillOpacity})`;
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // DNA Helix
  const renderDNAHelix = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    const centerX = width / 2;
    
    let offset = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'black';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update animation
      if (isAnimating) {
        offset += 0.02;
      }
      
      const amplitude = 80;
      const frequency = 0.02;
      const step = 5;
      const strandSeparation = 20;
      
      // Draw helix
      for (let y = 0; y < height + step; y += step) {
        // Calculate sine wave positions
        const x1 = centerX + Math.sin((y * frequency) + offset) * amplitude;
        const x2 = centerX + Math.sin((y * frequency) + offset + Math.PI) * amplitude;
        
        // Draw main strands
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(x1, y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = '#ff3366';
        ctx.fill();
        
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(x2, y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = '#3366ff';
        ctx.fill();
        
        // Draw connecting lines at intervals
        if (y % 20 < step) {
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(x1, y);
          ctx.lineTo(x2, y);
          ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(200, 200, 200, 0.5)';
          ctx.lineWidth = 2;
          ctx.stroke();
        }
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Aurora effect
  const renderAurora = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Aurora waves
    const waves = [];
    const waveCount = 5;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < waveCount; i++) {
      waves.push({
        points: [],
        color: `hsla(${120 + i * 30}, 80%, 60%, 0.2)`,
        speed: 0.003 + i * 0.001,
        offset: i * 0.2
      });
      
      // Generate points for each wave
      const pointCount = Math.floor(width / 10);
      for (let j = 0; j < pointCount; j++) {
        waves[i].points.push({
          x: j * (width / (pointCount - 1)),
          y: 0,
          noiseOffset: Math.random() * 100
        });
      }
    }
    
    let time = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Background gradient
      const gradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, height);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, '#000510');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, '#001030');
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update animation time
      if (isAnimating) {
        time += 0.01;
      }
      
      // Draw stars
      for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
        const x = i * (width / 100) + Math.sin(time + i * 0.1) * 1;
        const y = (i % 20) * (height / 20) + Math.cos(time + i * 0.1) * 1;
        const size = Math.random() * 2 + 0.5;
        
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(x, y, size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8)';
        ctx.fill();
      }
      
      // Draw waves from back to front
      waves.forEach(wave => {
        // Update points
        wave.points.forEach(point => {
          const noiseValue = Math.sin(point.x * 0.02 + time * wave.speed + wave.offset);
          const waveHeight = height * 0.5;
          point.y = height * 0.7 + noiseValue * waveHeight;
        });
        
        // Draw wave
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(0, height);
        ctx.lineTo(wave.points[0].x, wave.points[0].y);
        
        for (let i = 1; i < wave.points.length; i++) {
          const xc = (wave.points[i].x + wave.points[i - 1].x) / 2;
          const yc = (wave.points[i].y + wave.points[i - 1].y) / 2;
          ctx.quadraticCurveTo(wave.points[i - 1].x, wave.points[i - 1].y, xc, yc);
        }
        
        ctx.lineTo(width, wave.points[wave.points.length - 1].y);
        ctx.lineTo(width, height);
        ctx.closePath();
        
        // Fill with gradient based on wave color
        const waveGradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, height);
        const baseColor = wave.color.substring(0, wave.color.lastIndexOf(',')) + ',';
        waveGradient.addColorStop(0, baseColor + ' 0.8)');
        waveGradient.addColorStop(1, baseColor + ' 0)');
        
        ctx.fillStyle = waveGradient;
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Initialize the current effect
  useEffect(() => {
    let effectInitializer;
    
    switch(activeEffect) {
      case 'galaxy':
        effectInitializer = renderGalaxy;
        break;
      case 'fire-text':
        effectInitializer = renderFireText;
        break;
      case 'particle-explosion':
        effectInitializer = renderParticleExplosion;
        break;
      case 'data-flow':
        effectInitializer = renderDataFlow;
        break;
      case 'glitch-text':
        effectInitializer = renderGlitchText;
        break;
      case 'morphing-text':
        effectInitializer = renderMorphingText;
        break;
      case '3d-sphere':
        effectInitializer = render3DSphere;
        break;
      case 'dna-helix':
        effectInitializer = renderDNAHelix;
        break;
      case 'aurora':
        effectInitializer = renderAurora;
        break;
    }
    
    if (effectInitializer) {
      effectInitializer();
    }
    
    return () => {
      if (animationRef.current) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);
      }
    };
  }, [activeEffect, isAnimating]);
  
  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 space-y-8">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Premium Particle & Text Effects</h1>
        
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-6">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('galaxy')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'galaxy' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Galaxy Simulation
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('fire-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'fire-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Fire Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('particle-explosion')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'particle-explosion' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Particle Explosion
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('data-flow')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'data-flow' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Data Flow Network
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('glitch-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'glitch-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Glitch Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('morphing-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'morphing-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Morphing Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('3d-sphere')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === '3d-sphere' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            3D Particle Sphere
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('dna-helix')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'dna-helix' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            DNA Helix
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('aurora')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'aurora' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Aurora Effect
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mb-4">
          <button 
            onClick={triggerAnimation} 
            className="px-6 py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors"
          >
            Preview Animation
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="border border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-100 min-h-64">
          <canvas 
            ref={canvasRef}
            width="800"
            height="400"
            className="w-full h-64 bg-black rounded"
          ></canvas>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Current Effect: {activeEffect}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-700">
            {activeEffect === 'galaxy' && 'A simulated galaxy with thousands of particles rotating around a central point with realistic physics and color gradients.'}
            {activeEffect === 'fire-text' && 'Text revealed through rising fire particles with realistic physics and color gradation from yellow to red.'}
            {activeEffect === 'particle-explosion' && 'Thousands of particles exploding outward with gravity and realistic motion, creating a spectacular burst effect.'}
            {activeEffect === 'data-flow' && 'Visualization of data flowing through a network with nodes and connections, perfect for tech interfaces.'}
            {activeEffect === 'glitch-text' && 'Text with advanced digital distortion effects including RGB shifting, scan lines, and noise for a cyberpunk aesthetic.'}
            {activeEffect === 'morphing-text' && 'Text that smoothly morphs between different words with individual points transforming in sequence.'}
            {activeEffect === '3d-sphere' && 'A 3D sphere of particles with realistic perspective, rotation, and depth-based coloring.'}
            {activeEffect === 'dna-helix' && 'A double-helix DNA animation with connecting strands and smooth rotation for scientific visualization.'}
            {activeEffect === 'aurora' && 'Simulated northern lights with flowing waves of color against a starry night sky background.'}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default PremiumParticleEffects;

import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';

const PremiumParticleEffects = () => {
  const [activeEffect, setActiveEffect] = useState('galaxy');
  const [isAnimating, setIsAnimating] = useState(false);
  const animationRef = useRef(null);
  const canvasRef = useRef(null);
  
  // Animation control
  const triggerAnimation = () => {
    setIsAnimating(true);
    setTimeout(() => setIsAnimating(false), 4000);
  };
  
  // Cancel animation when switching effects
  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      if (animationRef.current) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);
      }
    };
  }, [activeEffect]);
  
  // Galaxy particle system
  const renderGalaxy = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const centerX = canvas.width / 2;
    const centerY = canvas.height / 2;
    
    let particles = [];
    const particleCount = 2000;
    
    // Create particles
    for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
      const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
      const radius = Math.random() * 150;
      const spread = Math.random() * 0.3;
      const armOffset = (Math.random() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1) * spread;
      
      const x = centerX + Math.cos(angle + armOffset) * radius;
      const y = centerY + Math.sin(angle + armOffset) * radius;
      
      // Hue based on position in galaxy (creates spiral color pattern)
      const hue = (angle / (Math.PI * 2)) * 360;
      
      particles.push({
        x,
        y,
        radius: Math.random() * 2 + 0.5,
        angle,
        armOffset,
        distFromCenter: radius,
        hue,
        originalX: x,
        originalY: y,
        velocity: 0.01 + Math.random() * 0.01
      });
    }
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(10, 10, 20, 0.1)';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
      
      // Draw black hole at center
      const gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(centerX, centerY, 0, centerX, centerY, 30);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(30, 30, 80, 0.8)');
      gradient.addColorStop(0.5, 'rgba(20, 20, 50, 0.4)');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0, 0, 20, 0)');
      
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.arc(centerX, centerY, 30, 0, Math.PI * 2);
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fill();
      
      // Draw particles
      particles.forEach(particle => {
        if (isAnimating) {
          // Update particle position
          particle.angle += particle.velocity * (1 - particle.distFromCenter / 200);
          particle.x = centerX + Math.cos(particle.angle + particle.armOffset) * particle.distFromCenter;
          particle.y = centerY + Math.sin(particle.angle + particle.armOffset) * particle.distFromCenter;
        }
        
        // Draw particle
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(particle.x, particle.y, particle.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${particle.hue}, 80%, 70%, 0.8)`;
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Fire text effect
  const renderFireText = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Create text
    ctx.font = 'bold 40px Arial';
    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
    ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
    
    const text = 'FIRE TEXT';
    const textMeasure = ctx.measureText(text);
    const textWidth = textMeasure.width;
    
    // Create text mask
    ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
    const textData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
    
    // Fire particle system
    const particles = [];
    const particleCount = 2000;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
      const x = Math.random() * width;
      const y = height + Math.random() * 20;
      
      particles.push({
        x,
        y,
        radius: Math.random() * 2 + 1,
        color: `hsl(${Math.random() * 30 + 15}, 100%, ${Math.random() * 30 + 50}%)`,
        vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 2,
        vy: -Math.random() * 5 - 2
      });
    }
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Create a fade effect
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        particles.forEach(particle => {
          // Update particle position
          particle.x += particle.vx;
          particle.y += particle.vy;
          
          // Check if particle is inside text
          const pixelIndex = (Math.floor(particle.y) * width + Math.floor(particle.x)) * 4;
          const alpha = textData.data[pixelIndex + 3];
          
          if (alpha > 0) {
            particle.radius *= 0.9;
          }
          
          // Draw particle
          if (particle.radius > 0.1) {
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(particle.x, particle.y, particle.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.fillStyle = particle.color;
            ctx.fill();
          }
          
          // Reset particles that go off screen or get too small
          if (particle.y < 0 || particle.radius <= 0.1) {
            particle.x = Math.random() * width;
            particle.y = height + Math.random() * 20;
            particle.radius = Math.random() * 2 + 1;
            particle.color = `hsl(${Math.random() * 30 + 15}, 100%, ${Math.random() * 30 + 50}%)`;
          }
        });
      } else {
        // Draw static text when not animating
        ctx.font = 'bold 40px Arial';
        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
        ctx.fillStyle = '#ff6600';
        ctx.fillText('FIRE TEXT', width / 2, height / 2);
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Particle explosion
  const renderParticleExplosion = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    const centerX = width / 2;
    const centerY = height / 2;
    
    const particles = [];
    const particleCount = 1000;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
      const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
      const speed = Math.random() * 6 + 2;
      
      particles.push({
        x: centerX,
        y: centerY,
        radius: Math.random() * 3 + 1,
        color: `hsl(${Math.random() * 360}, 80%, 60%)`,
        vx: Math.cos(angle) * speed,
        vy: Math.sin(angle) * speed,
        life: 1,
        decay: Math.random() * 0.01 + 0.005
      });
    }
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        particles.forEach(particle => {
          // Update particle
          particle.x += particle.vx;
          particle.y += particle.vy;
          particle.vy += 0.1; // Gravity
          particle.life -= particle.decay;
          
          // Draw particle
          if (particle.life > 0) {
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(particle.x, particle.y, particle.radius * particle.life, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.fillStyle = particle.color;
            ctx.globalAlpha = particle.life;
            ctx.fill();
            ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
          }
        });
      } else {
        // Draw static text
        ctx.font = 'bold 30px Arial';
        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
        ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
        ctx.fillText('CLICK TO EXPLODE', centerX, centerY);
      }
      
      // Reset particles if all are dead
      if (isAnimating && particles.every(p => p.life <= 0)) {
        particles.forEach(particle => {
          const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
          const speed = Math.random() * 6 + 2;
          
          particle.x = centerX;
          particle.y = centerY;
          particle.vx = Math.cos(angle) * speed;
          particle.vy = Math.sin(angle) * speed;
          particle.life = 1;
        });
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Data flow particles
  const renderDataFlow = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Create digital circuit pattern
    const nodes = [];
    const connections = [];
    const nodeCount = 20;
    
    // Generate nodes (connection points)
    for (let i = 0; i < nodeCount; i++) {
      nodes.push({
        x: Math.random() * width,
        y: Math.random() * height,
        radius: Math.random() * 3 + 2
      });
    }
    
    // Generate connections between nodes
    for (let i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) {
      // Each node connects to 1-3 other nodes
      const connectionCount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
      
      for (let j = 0; j < connectionCount; j++) {
        // Find a random node to connect to
        const targetIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * nodes.length);
        if (targetIndex !== i) {
          connections.push({
            source: i,
            target: targetIndex,
            particles: [],
            pulseTime: Math.random() * 2000 + 1000
          });
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Generate particles for each connection
    connections.forEach(connection => {
      const particleCount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 5) + 3;
      for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
        connection.particles.push({
          position: Math.random(),
          speed: Math.random() * 0.01 + 0.003,
          size: Math.random() * 2 + 1
        });
      }
    });
    
    let lastTime = 0;
    
    const animate = (time) => {
      const deltaTime = time - lastTime;
      lastTime = time;
      
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Draw connections
      connections.forEach(connection => {
        const source = nodes[connection.source];
        const target = nodes[connection.target];
        
        // Draw connection line
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(source.x, source.y);
        ctx.lineTo(target.x, target.y);
        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(50, 130, 230, 0.2)';
        ctx.lineWidth = 1;
        ctx.stroke();
        
        // Calculate distance and angle
        const dx = target.x - source.x;
        const dy = target.y - source.y;
        const distance = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
        
        // Update and draw particles
        if (isAnimating) {
          connection.particles.forEach(particle => {
            // Update particle position
            particle.position += particle.speed;
            if (particle.position > 1) particle.position = 0;
            
            // Calculate position
            const x = source.x + dx * particle.position;
            const y = source.y + dy * particle.position;
            
            // Draw particle
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(x, y, particle.size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.fillStyle = '#00aaff';
            ctx.fill();
          });
        }
      });
      
      // Draw nodes
      nodes.forEach(node => {
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(node.x, node.y, node.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = '#005588';
        ctx.fill();
        
        // Glow effect
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(node.x, node.y, node.radius + 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 170, 255, 0.2)';
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate(0);
  };
  
  // Glitch text effect
  const renderGlitchText = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    const text = 'GLITCH';
    
    // Slice data for glitch effect
    const slices = [];
    const sliceCount = 20;
    const sliceHeight = height / sliceCount;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < sliceCount; i++) {
      slices.push({
        y: i * sliceHeight,
        offset: 0,
        glitchTime: 0,
        glitchDuration: 0
      });
    }
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'black';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Render text
      ctx.font = 'bold 60px "Courier New", monospace';
      ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        // Update glitch animation
        slices.forEach(slice => {
          slice.glitchTime--;
          
          if (slice.glitchTime <= 0) {
            // New glitch
            if (Math.random() < 0.1) {
              slice.glitchTime = Math.floor(Math.random() * 20) + 5;
              slice.glitchDuration = slice.glitchTime;
              slice.offset = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 40;
            }
          }
          
          // Draw slice
          ctx.save();
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.rect(0, slice.y, width, sliceHeight);
          ctx.clip();
          
          // RGB shift
          if (slice.glitchTime > 0) {
            const progress = slice.glitchTime / slice.glitchDuration;
            
            // Red channel
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgb(255, 0, 0)';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2 + slice.offset * progress, height / 2);
            
            // Green channel
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgb(0, 255, 0)';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
            
            // Blue channel
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgb(0, 0, 255)';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2 - slice.offset * progress, height / 2);
          } else {
            // Normal rendering
            ctx.fillStyle = 'white';
            ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
          }
          
          ctx.restore();
        });
        
        // Random noise
        if (Math.random() < 0.1) {
          for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
            const noiseX = Math.random() * width;
            const noiseY = Math.random() * height;
            const noiseW = Math.random() * 40 + 10;
            const noiseH = Math.random() * 5 + 2;
            
            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.5)';
            ctx.fillRect(noiseX, noiseY, noiseW, noiseH);
          }
        }
      } else {
        // Static display
        ctx.fillStyle = 'white';
        ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Morphing text effect
  const renderMorphingText = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Text to morph between
    const words = ['MORPH', 'TEXT', 'EFFECT'];
    let currentIndex = 0;
    let nextIndex = 1;
    let progress = 0;
    const morphSpeed = 0.01;
    
    // Generate points for text
    const generateTextPoints = (text) => {
      ctx.font = 'bold 80px Arial';
      ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
      
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      ctx.fillText(text, width / 2, height / 2);
      
      const imageData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
      const pixels = imageData.data;
      const points = [];
      
      // Sample points
      const sampleSize = 3;
      for (let y = 0; y < height; y += sampleSize) {
        for (let x = 0; x < width; x += sampleSize) {
          const i = (y * width + x) * 4;
          if (pixels[i + 3] > 128) { // If pixel is opaque enough
            points.push({
              x,
              y,
              originX: x,
              originY: y
            });
          }
        }
      }
      
      return points;
    };
    
    let sourcePoints = generateTextPoints(words[currentIndex]);
    let targetPoints = generateTextPoints(words[nextIndex]);
    
    // Match point counts
    const matchPointCounts = () => {
      // Make source and target have the same number of points
      const minPoints = Math.min(sourcePoints.length, targetPoints.length);
      const maxPoints = Math.max(sourcePoints.length, targetPoints.length);
      
      if (sourcePoints.length < targetPoints.length) {
        // Add random existing points to source
        for (let i = minPoints; i < maxPoints; i++) {
          const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * minPoints);
          sourcePoints.push({ ...sourcePoints[randomIndex] });
        }
      } else if (targetPoints.length < sourcePoints.length) {
        // Add random existing points to target
        for (let i = minPoints; i < maxPoints; i++) {
          const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * minPoints);
          targetPoints.push({ ...targetPoints[randomIndex] });
        }
      }
    };
    
    matchPointCounts();
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      if (isAnimating) {
        // Update progress
        progress += morphSpeed;
        
        if (progress >= 1) {
          progress = 0;
          currentIndex = nextIndex;
          nextIndex = (nextIndex + 1) % words.length;
          sourcePoints = targetPoints;
          targetPoints = generateTextPoints(words[nextIndex]);
          matchPointCounts();
        }
        
        // Draw morphing points
        ctx.fillStyle = '#3366ff';
        
        for (let i = 0; i < sourcePoints.length; i++) {
          const source = sourcePoints[i];
          const target = targetPoints[i];
          
          const x = source.x + (target.x - source.x) * progress;
          const y = source.y + (target.y - source.y) * progress;
          
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.arc(x, y, 1.5, 0, Math.PI * 2);
          ctx.fill();
        }
      } else {
        // Static display
        ctx.font = 'bold 80px Arial';
        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
        ctx.fillStyle = '#3366ff';
        ctx.fillText('MORPHING', width / 2, height / 2);
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // 3D particle sphere
  const render3DSphere = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    const centerX = width / 2;
    const centerY = height / 2;
    
    // Generate sphere points
    const points = [];
    const radius = 100;
    const resolution = 30;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < 800; i++) {
      // Random point on sphere using spherical coordinates
      const theta = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
      const phi = Math.acos(2 * Math.random() - 1);
      
      const x = radius * Math.sin(phi) * Math.cos(theta);
      const y = radius * Math.sin(phi) * Math.sin(theta);
      const z = radius * Math.cos(phi);
      
      points.push({ x, y, z, size: Math.random() * 2 + 1 });
    }
    
    let rotation = 0;
    let tiltX = 0;
    let tiltY = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update rotation
      if (isAnimating) {
        rotation += 0.005;
        tiltX = Math.sin(rotation * 0.5) * 0.3;
        tiltY = Math.cos(rotation * 0.5) * 0.2;
      }
      
      // Clear with gradient background
      const gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(centerX, centerY, 0, centerX, centerY, radius * 1.5);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(30, 30, 70, 1)');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(10, 10, 30, 1)');
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Sort points by z-index for correct drawing order
      const sortedPoints = [...points].sort((a, b) => {
        // Apply rotation transformations to z for sorting
        const cosRY = Math.cos(rotation);
        const sinRY = Math.sin(rotation);
        const cosRX = Math.cos(tiltX);
        const sinRX = Math.sin(tiltX);
        
        const aRotZ = a.z * cosRY - a.x * sinRY;
        const bRotZ = b.z * cosRY - b.x * sinRY;
        
        return aRotZ - bRotZ;
      });
      
      // Draw points
      sortedPoints.forEach(point => {
        // Apply rotation transformations
        const cosRY = Math.cos(rotation);
        const sinRY = Math.sin(rotation);
        const cosRX = Math.cos(tiltX);
        const sinRX = Math.sin(tiltX);
        
        // Rotate around Y axis
        const x1 = point.x * cosRY + point.z * sinRY;
        const z1 = point.z * cosRY - point.x * sinRY;
        
        // Rotate around X axis
        const y2 = point.y * cosRX + z1 * sinRX;
        const z2 = z1 * cosRX - point.y * sinRX;
        
        // Project 3D point to 2D screen
        const scale = 1000 / (1000 + z2);
        const projX = centerX + x1 * scale;
        const projY = centerY + y2 * scale;
        
        // Draw point with size and color based on depth
        const fillOpacity = 0.2 + 0.8 * ((z2 + radius) / (radius * 2));
        const glowOpacity = 0.1 + 0.3 * ((z2 + radius) / (radius * 2));
        const hue = (((z2 + radius) / (radius * 2)) * 120) + 180;
        
        // Glow effect
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(projX, projY, point.size * scale * 2, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${hue}, 100%, 70%, ${glowOpacity})`;
        ctx.fill();
        
        // Core of point
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(projX, projY, point.size * scale, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${hue}, 100%, 70%, ${fillOpacity})`;
