        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // DNA Helix
  const renderDNAHelix = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    const centerX = width / 2;
    
    let offset = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'black';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update animation
      if (isAnimating) {
        offset += 0.02;
      }
      
      const amplitude = 80;
      const frequency = 0.02;
      const step = 5;
      const strandSeparation = 20;
      
      // Draw helix
      for (let y = 0; y < height + step; y += step) {
        // Calculate sine wave positions
        const x1 = centerX + Math.sin((y * frequency) + offset) * amplitude;
        const x2 = centerX + Math.sin((y * frequency) + offset + Math.PI) * amplitude;
        
        // Draw main strands
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(x1, y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = '#ff3366';
        ctx.fill();
        
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(x2, y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = '#3366ff';
        ctx.fill();
        
        // Draw connecting lines at intervals
        if (y % 20 < step) {
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(x1, y);
          ctx.lineTo(x2, y);
          ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(200, 200, 200, 0.5)';
          ctx.lineWidth = 2;
          ctx.stroke();
        }
      }
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Aurora effect
  const renderAurora = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth;
    canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
    
    const width = canvas.width;
    const height = canvas.height;
    
    // Aurora waves
    const waves = [];
    const waveCount = 5;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < waveCount; i++) {
      waves.push({
        points: [],
        color: `hsla(${120 + i * 30}, 80%, 60%, 0.2)`,
        speed: 0.003 + i * 0.001,
        offset: i * 0.2
      });
      
      // Generate points for each wave
      const pointCount = Math.floor(width / 10);
      for (let j = 0; j < pointCount; j++) {
        waves[i].points.push({
          x: j * (width / (pointCount - 1)),
          y: 0,
          noiseOffset: Math.random() * 100
        });
      }
    }
    
    let time = 0;
    
    const animate = () => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Background gradient
      const gradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, height);
      gradient.addColorStop(0, '#000510');
      gradient.addColorStop(1, '#001030');
      ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
      
      // Update animation time
      if (isAnimating) {
        time += 0.01;
      }
      
      // Draw stars
      for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
        const x = i * (width / 100) + Math.sin(time + i * 0.1) * 1;
        const y = (i % 20) * (height / 20) + Math.cos(time + i * 0.1) * 1;
        const size = Math.random() * 2 + 0.5;
        
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(x, y, size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8)';
        ctx.fill();
      }
      
      // Draw waves from back to front
      waves.forEach(wave => {
        // Update points
        wave.points.forEach(point => {
          const noiseValue = Math.sin(point.x * 0.02 + time * wave.speed + wave.offset);
          const waveHeight = height * 0.5;
          point.y = height * 0.7 + noiseValue * waveHeight;
        });
        
        // Draw wave
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(0, height);
        ctx.lineTo(wave.points[0].x, wave.points[0].y);
        
        for (let i = 1; i < wave.points.length; i++) {
          const xc = (wave.points[i].x + wave.points[i - 1].x) / 2;
          const yc = (wave.points[i].y + wave.points[i - 1].y) / 2;
          ctx.quadraticCurveTo(wave.points[i - 1].x, wave.points[i - 1].y, xc, yc);
        }
        
        ctx.lineTo(width, wave.points[wave.points.length - 1].y);
        ctx.lineTo(width, height);
        ctx.closePath();
        
        // Fill with gradient based on wave color
        const waveGradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, height);
        const baseColor = wave.color.substring(0, wave.color.lastIndexOf(',')) + ',';
        waveGradient.addColorStop(0, baseColor + ' 0.8)');
        waveGradient.addColorStop(1, baseColor + ' 0)');
        
        ctx.fillStyle = waveGradient;
        ctx.fill();
      });
      
      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    };
    
    animate();
  };
  
  // Initialize the current effect
  useEffect(() => {
    let effectInitializer;
    
    switch(activeEffect) {
      case 'galaxy':
        effectInitializer = renderGalaxy;
        break;
      case 'fire-text':
        effectInitializer = renderFireText;
        break;
      case 'particle-explosion':
        effectInitializer = renderParticleExplosion;
        break;
      case 'data-flow':
        effectInitializer = renderDataFlow;
        break;
      case 'glitch-text':
        effectInitializer = renderGlitchText;
        break;
      case 'morphing-text':
        effectInitializer = renderMorphingText;
        break;
      case '3d-sphere':
        effectInitializer = render3DSphere;
        break;
      case 'dna-helix':
        effectInitializer = renderDNAHelix;
        break;
      case 'aurora':
        effectInitializer = renderAurora;
        break;
    }
    
    if (effectInitializer) {
      effectInitializer();
    }
    
    return () => {
      if (animationRef.current) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);
      }
    };
  }, [activeEffect, isAnimating]);
  
  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 space-y-8">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Premium Particle & Text Effects</h1>
        
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-6">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('galaxy')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'galaxy' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Galaxy Simulation
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('fire-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'fire-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Fire Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('particle-explosion')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'particle-explosion' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Particle Explosion
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('data-flow')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'data-flow' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Data Flow Network
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('glitch-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'glitch-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Glitch Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('morphing-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'morphing-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Morphing Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('3d-sphere')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === '3d-sphere' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            3D Particle Sphere
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('dna-helix')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'dna-helix' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            DNA Helix
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('aurora')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'aurora' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Aurora Effect
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mb-4">
          <button 
            onClick={triggerAnimation} 
            className="px-6 py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors"
          >
            Preview Animation
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="border border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-100 min-h-64">
          <canvas 
            ref={canvasRef}
            width="800"
            height="400"
            className="w-full h-64 bg-black rounded"
          ></canvas>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Current Effect: {activeEffect}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-700">
            {activeEffect === 'galaxy' && 'A simulated galaxy with thousands of particles rotating around a central point with realistic physics and color gradients.'}
            {activeEffect === 'fire-text' && 'Text revealed through rising fire particles with realistic physics and color gradation from yellow to red.'}
            {activeEffect === 'particle-explosion' && 'Thousands of particles exploding outward with gravity and realistic motion, creating a spectacular burst effect.'}
            {activeEffect === 'data-flow' && 'Visualization of data flowing through a network with nodes and connections, perfect for tech interfaces.'}
            {activeEffect === 'glitch-text' && 'Text with advanced digital distortion effects including RGB shifting, scan lines, and noise for a cyberpunk aesthetic.'}
            {activeEffect === 'morphing-text' && 'Text that smoothly morphs between different words with individual points transforming in sequence.'}
            {activeEffect === '3d-sphere' && 'A 3D sphere of particles with realistic perspective, rotation, and depth-based coloring.'}
            {activeEffect === 'dna-helix' && 'A double-helix DNA animation with connecting strands and smooth rotation for scientific visualization.'}
            {activeEffect === 'aurora' && 'Simulated northern lights with flowing waves of color against a starry night sky background.'}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default PremiumParticleEffects;


import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

const AdvancedParticleEffects = () => {
  const [activeEffect, setActiveEffect] = useState('particle-swarm');
  const [isAnimating, setIsAnimating] = useState(false);
  const [animationFrame, setAnimationFrame] = useState(0);
  
  // Animation control
  const triggerAnimation = () => {
    setIsAnimating(true);
    setTimeout(() => setIsAnimating(false), 3000);
  };
  
  // Animation frame counter for continuous animations
  useEffect(() => {
    let frameId;
    if (isAnimating) {
      const animate = () => {
        setAnimationFrame(prev => prev + 1);
        frameId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
      };
      frameId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    }
    return () => {
      if (frameId) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(frameId);
      }
    };
  }, [isAnimating]);
  
  // Effect components
  const renderEffect = () => {
    switch(activeEffect) {
      case 'particle-swarm':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            {isAnimating && Array(50).fill().map((_, i) => {
              // Calculate particle properties
              const size = Math.random() * 8 + 2;
              const startX = Math.random() * 300 - 150;
              const startY = Math.random() * 300 - 150;
              const endX = Math.random() * 10 - 5;
              const endY = Math.random() * 10 - 5;
              const duration = Math.random() * 2 + 1;
              const delay = Math.random() * 0.5;
              const opacity = Math.random() * 0.6 + 0.4;
              
              return (
                <div 
                  key={i}
                  className="absolute rounded-full bg-blue-500"
                  style={{
                    width: `${size}px`,
                    height: `${size}px`,
                    left: 'calc(50% + 0px)',
                    top: 'calc(50% + 0px)',
                    opacity: opacity,
                    transform: `translate(${startX}px, ${startY}px)`,
                    transition: `transform ${duration}s ease-out ${delay}s`
                  }}
                >
                  <div 
                    className="w-full h-full rounded-full bg-blue-500 transition-transform"
                    style={{
                      transform: `translate(${endX}px, ${endY}px)`,
                      transition: `transform ${duration * 4}s ease-in-out`,
                      boxShadow: '0 0 4px rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.5)'
                    }}
                  />
                </div>
              );
            })}
            <div className="text-xl font-bold text-blue-600 z-10">Particle Swarm</div>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'fluid-simulation':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <svg width="100%" height="100%" viewBox="0 0 400 200">
              <defs>
                <linearGradient id="fluid-gradient" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
                  <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#2563eb" />
                  <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#7c3aed" />
                </linearGradient>
                <filter id="fluid-turbulence">
                  <feTurbulence 
                    type="fractalNoise" 
                    baseFrequency="0.01 0.01" 
                    seed="3" 
                    numOctaves="3" 
                    result="turbulence"
                    stitchTiles="stitch"
                  >
                    <animate 
                      attributeName="baseFrequency" 
                      values="0.01 0.01;0.02 0.02;0.01 0.01" 
                      dur="10s" 
                      repeatCount="indefinite"
                      begin={isAnimating ? "0s" : "indefinite"}
                    />
                  </feTurbulence>
                  <feDisplacementMap in="SourceGraphic" in2="turbulence" scale="30" xChannelSelector="R" yChannelSelector="G" />
                </filter>
              </defs>
              <g filter={isAnimating ? "url(#fluid-turbulence)" : ""}>
                <rect x="50" y="50" width="300" height="100" rx="20" fill="url(#fluid-gradient)" />
                <text x="200" y="105" textAnchor="middle" fill="white" fontSize="20" fontWeight="bold">
                  Fluid Distortion
                </text>
              </g>
            </svg>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'constellation':
        const numNodes = 12;
        const nodes = [];
        const connections = [];
        
        // Create nodes with fixed positions for consistency
        for (let i = 0; i < numNodes; i++) {
          const angle = (i / numNodes) * Math.PI * 2;
          const radius = Math.random() * 40 + 60;
          const x = Math.cos(angle) * radius + 150;
          const y = Math.sin(angle) * radius + 100;
          nodes.push({ id: i, x, y });
        }
        
        // Create connections between nodes
        for (let i = 0; i < numNodes; i++) {
          for (let j = i + 1; j < numNodes; j++) {
            const distance = Math.sqrt(
              Math.pow(nodes[i].x - nodes[j].x, 2) + 
              Math.pow(nodes[i].y - nodes[j].y, 2)
            );
            
            if (distance < 70) {
              connections.push({ 
                id: `${i}-${j}`, 
                source: i, 
                target: j, 
                distance 
              });
            }
          }
        }
        
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <svg width="100%" height="100%" viewBox="0 0 300 200">
              <g>
                {/* Draw connections */}
                {connections.map(conn => {
                  const source = nodes[conn.source];
                  const target = nodes[conn.target];
                  const opacity = isAnimating ? 
                    Math.max(0, 1 - (conn.distance / 100)) : 
                    Math.max(0, 0.5 - (conn.distance / 100));
                  
                  return (
                    <line 
                      key={conn.id}
                      x1={source.x} 
                      y1={source.y} 
                      x2={target.x} 
                      y2={target.y}
                      stroke="#4f46e5"
                      strokeWidth="1"
                      opacity={opacity}
                      className="transition-opacity duration-1000"
                    />
                  );
                })}
                
                {/* Draw nodes */}
                {nodes.map(node => (
                  <g key={node.id}>
                    <circle 
                      cx={node.x} 
                      cy={node.y} 
                      r={isAnimating ? 4 : 3}
                      fill={isAnimating ? "#3b82f6" : "#6366f1"}
                      className="transition-all duration-700"
                    />
                    {isAnimating && (
                      <circle 
                        cx={node.x} 
                        cy={node.y} 
                        r="8"
                        fill="none"
                        stroke="#93c5fd"
                        strokeWidth="1"
                        opacity="0.5"
                        className="animate-ping"
                      />
                    )}
                  </g>
                ))}
              </g>
            </svg>
            <div className="absolute bottom-4 text-center w-full text-indigo-600 font-semibold">
              Network Constellation
            </div>
          </div>
        );
                
      case 'particle-text':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <svg width="100%" height="100%" viewBox="0 0 300 100">
              <defs>
                <filter id="particle-disintegration" x="-20%" y="-20%" width="140%" height="140%">
                  <feTurbulence type="fractalNoise" baseFrequency="0.05" numOctaves="1" result="noise" />
                  <feDisplacementMap 
                    in="SourceGraphic" 
                    in2="noise" 
                    scale={isAnimating ? "20" : "0"} 
                    xChannelSelector="R" 
                    yChannelSelector="G" 
                  >
                    <animate 
                      attributeName="scale" 
                      values="0;20;0" 
                      dur="3s" 
                      begin={isAnimating ? "0s" : "indefinite"}
                    />
                  </feDisplacementMap>
                </filter>
              </defs>
              <text 
                x="150" 
                y="60" 
                textAnchor="middle" 
                filter="url(#particle-disintegration)"
                fill="#3b82f6"
                fontWeight="bold"
                fontSize="32"
              >
                DISINTEGRATE
              </text>
            </svg>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'energy-field':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <div className="w-64 h-48 rounded-lg bg-indigo-900 flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold relative overflow-hidden">
              <div className="z-10 relative">Energy Field</div>
              
              {/* Energy field particles */}
              {isAnimating && Array(20).fill().map((_, i) => {
                const delay = i * 0.1;
                const size = Math.random() * 10 + 5;
                const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
                const distance = Math.random() * 30 + 40;
                const duration = Math.random() * 2 + 1;
                const x = Math.cos(angle) * distance;
                const y = Math.sin(angle) * distance;
                
                return (
                  <div 
                    key={i}
                    className="absolute rounded-full bg-blue-400 opacity-70"
                    style={{
                      width: `${size}px`,
                      height: `${size}px`,
                      left: 'calc(50% - 4px)',
                      top: 'calc(50% - 4px)',
                      boxShadow: '0 0 15px rgba(96, 165, 250, 0.7)',
                      animation: `pulse ${duration}s ease-in-out infinite alternate`,
                      transform: `translate(${x}px, ${y}px) scale(${isAnimating ? 1 : 0})`,
                      transition: `transform ${duration}s ease-out ${delay}s`
                    }}
                  />
                );
              })}
              
              {/* Central glow */}
              <div 
                className="absolute w-24 h-24 rounded-full bg-blue-400 opacity-30 transition-all duration-1000"
                style={{
                  filter: 'blur(10px)',
                  transform: isAnimating ? 'scale(1.5)' : 'scale(0.8)',
                  animation: isAnimating ? 'pulse 2s ease-in-out infinite alternate' : 'none'
                }}
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'matrix-effect':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden bg-black">
            <div className="absolute inset-0 font-mono text-green-500 text-opacity-70 leading-none text-sm overflow-hidden">
              {isAnimating && Array(30).fill().map((_, i) => {
                const column = i % 15;
                const speed = Math.random() * 300 + 700;
                const chars = "01アイウエオカキクケコサシスセソタチツテトナニヌネノ";
                
                return (
                  <div 
                    key={i}
                    className="absolute"
                    style={{
                      left: `${column * 30 + 10}px`,
                      top: 0,
                      animation: `matrixDrop ${speed}ms linear infinite`,
                      animationDelay: `${i * 100}ms`
                    }}
                  >
                    {Array(20).fill().map((_, j) => {
                      const randomChar = chars[Math.floor(Math.random() * chars.length)];
                      return (
                        <div key={j} className="leading-none my-2">
                          {randomChar}
                        </div>
                      );
                    })}
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>
            <div className="text-green-400 text-2xl font-bold z-10 text-center">
              <div className={isAnimating ? "animate-pulse" : ""}>MATRIX RAIN</div>
            </div>
            <style jsx>{`
              @keyframes matrixDrop {
                0% { transform: translateY(-100%); }
                100% { transform: translateY(100%); }
              }
              @keyframes pulse {
                0% { opacity: 0.3; }
                100% { opacity: 0.7; }
              }
            `}</style>
          </div>
        );

      case 'water-ripple':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <div className="w-64 h-48 bg-gradient-to-b from-blue-300 to-blue-600 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center relative overflow-hidden">
              <div className="text-white text-xl font-bold z-10">Water Ripple</div>
              
              {isAnimating && Array(4).fill().map((_, i) => {
                const delay = i * 0.6;
                
                return (
                  <div 
                    key={i}
                    className="absolute rounded-full border border-white border-opacity-50 transition-all"
                    style={{
                      width: '20px',
                      height: '20px',
                      left: 'calc(50% - 10px)',
                      top: 'calc(50% - 10px)',
                      transform: `scale(${isAnimating ? 8 : 0})`,
                      opacity: isAnimating ? 0 : 1,
                      transition: `transform 3s ease-out ${delay}s, opacity 3s ease-out ${delay}s`
                    }}
                  />
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'electric-pulse':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <svg width="100%" height="100%" viewBox="0 0 300 200">
              <defs>
                <filter id="glow" x="-20%" y="-20%" width="140%" height="140%">
                  <feGaussianBlur stdDeviation="5" result="blur" />
                  <feComposite in="SourceGraphic" in2="blur" operator="over" />
                </filter>
              </defs>
              
              {/* Path for the electric arc */}
              <path 
                d={`M 50,100 
                   C 70,${isAnimating ? 70 : 100} 90,${isAnimating ? 130 : 100} 110,${isAnimating ? 90 : 100} 
                   C 130,${isAnimating ? 50 : 100} 150,${isAnimating ? 150 : 100} 170,${isAnimating ? 70 : 100}
                   C 190,${isAnimating ? 90 : 100} 210,${isAnimating ? 110 : 100} 250,${isAnimating ? 80 : 100}`}
                stroke="#60a5fa"
                strokeWidth="3"
                fill="none"
                filter="url(#glow)"
                className="transition-all duration-300"
                strokeDasharray={isAnimating ? "5,5" : "none"}
                opacity={isAnimating ? "0.8" : "0.3"}
              />
              
              {/* Nodes at either end */}
              <circle cx="50" cy="100" r="10" fill="#3b82f6" filter="url(#glow)" />
              <circle cx="250" cy="100" r="10" fill="#3b82f6" filter="url(#glow)" />
              
              {/* Pulsing glow when active */}
              {isAnimating && (
                <>
                  <circle cx="50" cy="100" r="15" fill="none" stroke="#93c5fd" strokeWidth="2" className="animate-ping" />
                  <circle cx="250" cy="100" r="15" fill="none" stroke="#93c5fd" strokeWidth="2" className="animate-ping" />
                </>
              )}
            </svg>
            <div className="absolute bottom-4 text-center w-full text-blue-600 font-semibold">
              Electric Pulse
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'confetti-explosion':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <button 
              className={`px-6 py-3 bg-purple-600 text-white rounded-lg shadow-lg transition-all ${isAnimating ? 'scale-105' : ''}`}
            >
              Celebrate!
            </button>
            
            {/* Confetti pieces */}
            {isAnimating && Array(80).fill().map((_, i) => {
              const colors = ['#ef4444', '#f59e0b', '#3b82f6', '#10b981', '#8b5cf6', '#ec4899'];
              const color = colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length)];
              const size = Math.random() * 8 + 4;
              const isSquare = Math.random() > 0.5;
              const angle = Math.random() * 360;
              const distance = Math.random() * 150 + 30;
              const startAngle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
              const x = Math.cos(startAngle) * distance;
              const y = Math.sin(startAngle) * distance;
              const rotateSpeed = Math.random() * 760 + 360;
              const delay = Math.random() * 0.5;
              
              return (
                <div 
                  key={i}
                  className="absolute transition-all"
                  style={{
                    width: `${size}px`,
                    height: isSquare ? `${size}px` : `${size * 0.4}px`,
                    borderRadius: isSquare ? '2px' : '0',
                    backgroundColor: color,
                    left: 'calc(50% - 4px)',
                    top: 'calc(50% - 4px)',
                    opacity: isAnimating ? 1 : 0,
                    transform: `translate(${x}px, ${y}px) rotate(${angle}deg)`,
                    transition: `transform 1s ease-out ${delay}s, opacity 0.8s ease-out ${delay}s`,
                    animation: `spin ${rotateSpeed}ms linear infinite`
                  }}
                />
              );
            })}
            
            <style jsx>{`
              @keyframes spin {
                from { transform: translate(${isAnimating ? 'var(--x, 0)' : '0'}px, ${isAnimating ? 'var(--y, 0)' : '0'}px) rotate(0deg); }
                to { transform: translate(${isAnimating ? 'var(--x, 0)' : '0'}px, ${isAnimating ? 'var(--y, 0)' : '0'}px) rotate(360deg); }
              }
            `}</style>
          </div>
        );
        
      default:
        return <div>Select an effect</div>;
    }
  };
  
  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 space-y-8">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Advanced Particle & Complex Animation Effects</h1>
        
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-6">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('particle-swarm')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'particle-swarm' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Particle Swarm
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('fluid-simulation')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'fluid-simulation' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Fluid Simulation
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('constellation')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'constellation' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Constellation
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('particle-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'particle-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Particle Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('energy-field')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'energy-field' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Energy Field
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('matrix-effect')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'matrix-effect' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Matrix Rain
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('water-ripple')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'water-ripple' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Water Ripple
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('electric-pulse')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'electric-pulse' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Electric Pulse
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('confetti-explosion')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'confetti-explosion' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Confetti Explosion
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mb-4">
          <button 
            onClick={triggerAnimation} 
            className="px-6 py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors"
          >
            Preview Animation
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="border border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-100 min-h-64">
          {renderEffect()}
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Current Effect: {activeEffect}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-700">
            {activeEffect === 'particle-swarm' && 'Dynamic particles that move and swarm around a central point with independent behaviors. Creates organic, lifelike motion.'}
            {activeEffect === 'fluid-simulation' && 'SVG-based fluid distortion effect that mimics liquid movement. Creates an organic, flowing distortion of content.'}
            {activeEffect === 'constellation' && 'Interactive network of connected nodes that responds to interaction. Perfect for data visualization or abstract backgrounds.'}
            {activeEffect === 'particle-text' && 'Text that disintegrates into particles using SVG turbulence filters. Creates dramatic transitions for text elements.'}
            {activeEffect === 'energy-field' && 'Glowing particles that orbit around a central point with pulsing energy. Great for sci-fi interfaces or power indicators.'}
            {activeEffect === 'matrix-effect' && 'Falling characters animation inspired by "The Matrix" films. Creates a distinctive digital rain effect.'}
            {activeEffect === 'water-ripple' && 'Concentric circles that expand outward like ripples on water. Perfect for indicating interaction points or notifications.'}
            {activeEffect === 'electric-pulse' && 'Animated electric arc that connects two points with glowing energy. Visualizes connections or data transfer.'}
            {activeEffect === 'confetti-explosion' && 'Colorful confetti particles that burst outward in a celebration effect. Great for achievements or success states.'}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default AdvancedParticleEffects;

import React, { useState } from 'react';

const SpecializedAnimationEffects = () => {
  const [activeEffect, setActiveEffect] = useState('3d-cube');
  const [isAnimating, setIsAnimating] = useState(false);
  
  // Card data
  const cards = [
    { id: 1, color: 'bg-blue-500', title: 'Card 1' },
    { id: 2, color: 'bg-green-500', title: 'Card 2' },
    { id: 3, color: 'bg-yellow-500', title: 'Card 3' },
    { id: 4, color: 'bg-red-500', title: 'Card 4' },
    { id: 5, color: 'bg-purple-500', title: 'Card 5' }
  ];
  
  // Animation control
  const triggerAnimation = () => {
    setIsAnimating(true);
    setTimeout(() => setIsAnimating(false), 3000);
  };
  
  // Effect components
  const renderEffect = () => {
    switch(activeEffect) {
      case '3d-cube':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center perspective-1000">
            <div 
              className="w-48 h-48 relative preserve-3d transition-all duration-1500"
              style={{
                transform: isAnimating ? 'rotateY(360deg) rotateX(360deg)' : 'rotateY(0) rotateX(0)'
              }}
            >
              {/* Front face */}
              <div className="absolute w-full h-full bg-blue-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white"
                style={{ transform: 'translateZ(24px)' }}>
                Front
              </div>
              {/* Back face */}
              <div className="absolute w-full h-full bg-red-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white"
                style={{ transform: 'rotateY(180deg) translateZ(24px)' }}>
                Back
              </div>
              {/* Left face */}
              <div className="absolute w-full h-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white"
                style={{ transform: 'rotateY(-90deg) translateZ(24px)' }}>
                Left
              </div>
              {/* Right face */}
              <div className="absolute w-full h-full bg-yellow-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white"
                style={{ transform: 'rotateY(90deg) translateZ(24px)' }}>
                Right
              </div>
              {/* Top face */}
              <div className="absolute w-full h-full bg-purple-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white"
                style={{ transform: 'rotateX(90deg) translateZ(24px)' }}>
                Top
              </div>
              {/* Bottom face */}
              <div className="absolute w-full h-full bg-pink-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white"
                style={{ transform: 'rotateX(-90deg) translateZ(24px)' }}>
                Bottom
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'liquid-fill':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <div className="w-64 h-48 rounded-lg bg-transparent border-2 border-blue-500 overflow-hidden relative flex items-center justify-center">
              <div className="z-10 text-white font-bold relative">Liquid Fill</div>
              <div 
                className="absolute bottom-0 left-0 right-0 bg-blue-500 w-full transition-all duration-2000 ease-in-out"
                style={{ 
                  height: isAnimating ? '100%' : '0%',
                  borderRadius: '0 0 0.5rem 0.5rem'
                }}
              ></div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'typewriter':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <div className="text-2xl font-mono flex">
              <span>Welcome to&nbsp;</span>
              <span className="text-blue-600 relative">
                {isAnimating ? "Animation Effects" : ""}
                <span 
                  className="absolute top-0 left-0 bg-white w-0 h-full transition-all"
                  style={{ 
                    width: isAnimating ? '0%' : '100%',
                    transitionDuration: isAnimating ? '2s' : '0s',
                    transitionDelay: '0.5s'
                  }}
                ></span>
              </span>
              <span className={`ml-1 animate-ping ${isAnimating ? '' : 'hidden'}`}>|</span>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'perspective-tilt':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <div 
              className="w-64 h-48 rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-indigo-500 to-purple-600 text-white flex items-center justify-center text-xl font-bold shadow-lg transition-all duration-500"
              style={{
                transform: isAnimating ? 'perspective(500px) rotateX(10deg) rotateY(15deg)' : 'perspective(500px) rotateX(0) rotateY(0)',
                boxShadow: isAnimating ? '0 20px 25px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3)' : '0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2)'
              }}
            >
              3D Tilt
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'radial-reveal':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <div className="relative w-64 h-48 rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-400 to-purple-500 flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
              <div className="text-white text-xl font-bold z-10">Radial Reveal</div>
              <div 
                className="absolute inset-0 bg-black transition-all duration-1000 rounded-lg"
                style={{
                  clipPath: isAnimating ? 
                    'circle(100% at center)' : 
                    'circle(0% at center)'
                }}
              ></div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'magnetic-hover':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <div className="relative w-64 text-center">
              <div 
                className={`inline-block px-6 py-3 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-lg cursor-pointer transition-all duration-500 ${isAnimating ? 'transform scale-110' : ''}`}
              >
                Magnetic Button
              </div>
              <div 
                className={`absolute inset-0 pointer-events-none transition-opacity duration-700 ${isAnimating ? 'opacity-100' : 'opacity-0'}`}
              >
                {Array(8).fill().map((_, i) => {
                  const angle = (i * Math.PI * 2) / 8;
                  const x = Math.cos(angle) * 70;
                  const y = Math.sin(angle) * 25;
                  
                  return (
                    <div 
                      key={i}
                      className="absolute w-1 h-1 rounded-full bg-blue-400"
                      style={{
                        left: 'calc(50% + ' + x + 'px)',
                        top: 'calc(50% + ' + y + 'px)',
                        opacity: 0.6,
                        transform: isAnimating ? 'scale(1)' : 'scale(0)'
                      }}
                    ></div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'split-text':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <div className="relative">
              <div className="text-4xl font-bold text-transparent" style={{ WebkitTextStroke: '1px #4a5568' }}>
                SPLIT TEXT
              </div>
              <div 
                className="absolute inset-0 text-4xl font-bold text-blue-500 transition-transform duration-500 overflow-hidden"
                style={{
                  clipPath: 'polygon(0 0, 100% 0, 100% 50%, 0 50%)',
                  transform: isAnimating ? 'translateX(-10px)' : 'translateX(0)'
                }}
              >
                SPLIT TEXT
              </div>
              <div 
                className="absolute inset-0 text-4xl font-bold text-red-500 transition-transform duration-500 overflow-hidden"
                style={{
                  clipPath: 'polygon(0 50%, 100% 50%, 100% 100%, 0 100%)',
                  transform: isAnimating ? 'translateX(10px)' : 'translateX(0)'
                }}
              >
                SPLIT TEXT
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'image-mask-reveal':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <div 
              className="w-64 h-48 bg-gradient-to-r from-pink-500 to-purple-500 relative rounded-lg overflow-hidden"
            >
              <div 
                className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center transition-opacity duration-1000"
                style={{
                  opacity: isAnimating ? 1 : 0
                }}
              >
                <svg width="100%" height="100%" viewBox="0 0 100 100" preserveAspectRatio="none">
                  <defs>
                    <mask id="mask" x="0" y="0" width="100%" height="100%">
                      <rect x="0" y="0" width="100%" height="100%" fill="#fff"/>
                      <text 
                        x="50" 
                        y="50" 
                        textAnchor="middle" 
                        dominantBaseline="middle"
                        fill="#000" 
                        fontSize="15"
                        style={{
                          fontWeight: 'bold',
                          fontFamily: 'sans-serif'
                        }}
                      >
                        TEXT MASK
                      </text>
                    </mask>
                  </defs>
                  <rect x="0" y="0" width="100%" height="100%" fill="white" mask="url(#mask)" />
                </svg>
              </div>
              <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold opacity-70">
                Masked Content
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'wavy-text':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <div className="text-3xl font-bold">
              {"WAVE EFFECT".split('').map((char, i) => (
                <span 
                  key={i}
                  className="inline-block transition-transform duration-200"
                  style={{
                    transform: isAnimating ? `translateY(${Math.sin((i * 0.5) + (isAnimating ? Date.now() / 300 : 0)) * 10}px)` : 'translateY(0)',
                    color: `hsl(${i * 30}, 70%, 60%)`,
                    animationDelay: `${i * 0.05}s`
                  }}
                >
                  {char}
                </span>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        );
        
      default:
        return <div>Select an effect</div>;
    }
  };
  
  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 space-y-8">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Specialized UI Animation Effects</h1>
        
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-6">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('3d-cube')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === '3d-cube' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            3D Cube Rotation
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('liquid-fill')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'liquid-fill' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Liquid Fill
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('typewriter')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'typewriter' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Typewriter Effect
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('perspective-tilt')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'perspective-tilt' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Perspective Tilt
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('radial-reveal')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'radial-reveal' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Radial Reveal
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('magnetic-hover')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'magnetic-hover' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Magnetic Effect
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('split-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'split-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Split Text
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('image-mask-reveal')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'image-mask-reveal' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Mask Reveal
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('wavy-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'wavy-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Wavy Text
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mb-4">
          <button 
            onClick={triggerAnimation} 
            className="px-6 py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors"
          >
            Preview Animation
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="border border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-100 min-h-64">
          {renderEffect()}
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Current Effect: {activeEffect}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-700">
            {activeEffect === '3d-cube' && '3D cube rotation that shows content on all 6 faces. Creates an immersive spatial experience for content navigation.'}
            {activeEffect === 'liquid-fill' && 'Element fills with color like a liquid rising. Perfect for progress indicators or emphasizing completion.'}
            {activeEffect === 'typewriter' && 'Text appears character by character as if being typed. Creates focus and anticipation for important messages.'}
            {activeEffect === 'perspective-tilt' && '3D tilting effect that responds to interaction. Adds depth and tactile feel to interface elements.'}
            {activeEffect === 'radial-reveal' && 'Content revealed in a circular pattern expanding outward. Creates a focused point of attention.'}
            {activeEffect === 'magnetic-hover' && 'Elements appear to have magnetic properties, with particles or elements drawn toward them. Creates an interactive, playful experience.'}
            {activeEffect === 'split-text' && 'Text splits into layers that move independently. Creates a bold, glitch-like aesthetic for headers.'}
            {activeEffect === 'image-mask-reveal' && 'Content revealed through mask shapes or text. Creates unique visual interest and branded reveals.'}
            {activeEffect === 'wavy-text' && 'Text characters move in a wave-like pattern. Creates dynamic, fluid motion in typography.'}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default SpecializedAnimationEffects;

import React, { useState } from 'react';

const AdvancedAnimationEffects = () => {
  const [activeEffect, setActiveEffect] = useState('morph');
  const [isAnimating, setIsAnimating] = useState(false);
  
  // Card data
  const cards = [
    { id: 1, color: 'bg-blue-500', title: 'Card 1' },
    { id: 2, color: 'bg-green-500', title: 'Card 2' },
    { id: 3, color: 'bg-yellow-500', title: 'Card 3' },
    { id: 4, color: 'bg-red-500', title: 'Card 4' },
    { id: 5, color: 'bg-purple-500', title: 'Card 5' }
  ];
  
  // Animation control
  const triggerAnimation = () => {
    setIsAnimating(true);
    setTimeout(() => setIsAnimating(false), 3000);
  };
  
  // Effect components
  const renderEffect = () => {
    switch(activeEffect) {
      case 'morph':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <div 
              className={`w-64 h-48 flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg transition-all duration-1000 ${isAnimating ? 'rounded-full bg-purple-500' : 'rounded-lg bg-blue-500'}`}
              style={{
                transform: isAnimating ? 'rotate(360deg)' : 'rotate(0deg)'
              }}
            >
              {isAnimating ? 'Morphed!' : 'Shape Morph'}
            </div>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'parallax':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full overflow-hidden">
            <div 
              className="absolute w-full h-full bg-blue-200 flex items-center justify-center"
              style={{
                transform: isAnimating ? 'translateY(-10px)' : 'translateY(0px)',
                transition: 'transform 1s ease-out'
              }}
            >
              Background Layer
            </div>
            <div 
              className="absolute w-full h-full flex items-center justify-center opacity-30"
              style={{
                transform: isAnimating ? 'translateY(-20px)' : 'translateY(0px)',
                transition: 'transform 1s ease-out'
              }}
            >
              <div className="w-48 h-48 rounded-full bg-blue-400"></div>
            </div>
            <div 
              className="absolute w-full h-full flex items-center justify-center"
              style={{
                transform: isAnimating ? 'translateY(-40px)' : 'translateY(0px)',
                transition: 'transform 1s ease-out'
              }}
            >
              <div className="w-32 h-12 rounded-lg bg-blue-700 text-white flex items-center justify-center">
                Foreground
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'stagger-reveal':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center">
            {cards.slice(0, 5).map((card, index) => {
              // Calculate staggered reveal 
              const delay = index * 0.15;
              const offsetX = isAnimating ? '0px' : '100px';
              const opacity = isAnimating ? 1 : 0;
              
              return (
                <div 
                  key={card.id} 
                  className={`w-64 h-10 ${card.color} rounded mb-2 flex items-center justify-center text-white transition-all`}
                  style={{
                    transform: `translateX(${offsetX})`,
                    opacity: opacity,
                    transitionDelay: `${delay}s`,
                    transitionDuration: '0.5s'
                  }}
                >
                  {card.title}
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'fold-unfold':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <div 
              className="w-64 h-48 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-purple-500 rounded-lg shadow-lg overflow-hidden"
              style={{
                transformOrigin: 'top',
                transform: isAnimating ? 'perspective(800px) rotateX(0deg)' : 'perspective(800px) rotateX(-90deg)',
                transition: 'transform 1s ease-in-out'
              }}
            >
              <div className="w-full h-full flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl">
                Unfolding Panel
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'blur-reveal':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <div 
              className="w-64 h-48 bg-gradient-to-r from-green-400 to-blue-500 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold transition-all duration-1000"
              style={{
                filter: isAnimating ? 'blur(0px)' : 'blur(10px)',
                opacity: isAnimating ? 1 : 0.5,
                transform: isAnimating ? 'scale(1)' : 'scale(0.95)'
              }}
            >
              Sharp Focus
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'particle-reveal':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <div 
              className="w-64 h-48 rounded-lg bg-blue-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold z-10 relative transition-opacity duration-1000"
              style={{
                opacity: isAnimating ? 1 : 0
              }}
            >
              Content Revealed
            </div>
            
            {/* Particles */}
            {Array(20).fill().map((_, i) => {
              const size = Math.floor(Math.random() * 15) + 5;
              const initialX = Math.random() * 64 - 32;
              const initialY = Math.random() * 48 - 24;
              const finalX = (Math.random() * 300 - 150) + (initialX * 5);
              const finalY = (Math.random() * 300 - 150) + (initialY * 5);
              const delay = Math.random() * 0.5;
              const duration = Math.random() * 0.5 + 0.5;
              
              return (
                <div 
                  key={i}
                  className="absolute rounded-full bg-blue-400 z-0"
                  style={{
                    width: `${size}px`,
                    height: `${size}px`,
                    left: 'calc(50% - 32px)',
                    top: 'calc(50% - 24px)',
                    transform: isAnimating ? `translate(${finalX}px, ${finalY}px) scale(0)` : `translate(${initialX}px, ${initialY}px) scale(1)`,
                    opacity: isAnimating ? 0 : 0.8,
                    transition: `transform ${duration}s ease-out ${delay}s, opacity ${duration}s ease-out ${delay}s`
                  }}
                />
              );
            })}
          </div>
        );

      case 'swing-in':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <div 
              className="w-64 h-48 rounded-lg bg-amber-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold transition-all duration-1000"
              style={{
                transform: isAnimating ? 'rotate(0deg)' : 'rotate(-15deg) translateX(-150px)',
                transformOrigin: 'top left',
                transitionTimingFunction: 'cubic-bezier(.5,2,.8,1)'
              }}
            >
              Swing In
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'shutter-reveal':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <div className="w-64 h-48 rounded-lg bg-indigo-600 flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold relative overflow-hidden">
              Hidden Content
              
              {/* Top shutter */}
              <div 
                className="absolute inset-0 bg-gray-800 transition-transform duration-1000"
                style={{
                  height: '50%',
                  transformOrigin: 'top',
                  transform: isAnimating ? 'translateY(-100%)' : 'translateY(0)'
                }}
              />
              
              {/* Bottom shutter */}
              <div 
                className="absolute inset-0 bg-gray-800 top-1/2 transition-transform duration-1000"
                style={{
                  height: '50%',
                  transformOrigin: 'bottom',
                  transform: isAnimating ? 'translateY(100%)' : 'translateY(0)'
                }}
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'glitch-text':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            <div 
              className="text-3xl font-bold text-white relative"
              style={{
                textShadow: isAnimating ? '2px 0 #ff00ea, -2px 0 #00a2ff' : 'none',
                animation: isAnimating ? 'glitch 1s infinite' : 'none'
              }}
            >
              GLITCH EFFECT
              
              {isAnimating && (
                <>
                  <div 
                    className="absolute inset-0 text-red-500 hidden md:block"
                    style={{
                      animation: 'glitch-anim-1 2s infinite linear alternate',
                      clipPath: 'polygon(0 0, 100% 0, 100% 35%, 0 35%)',
                      transform: 'translateX(-2px)'
                    }}
                  >
                    GLITCH EFFECT
                  </div>
                  <div 
                    className="absolute inset-0 text-blue-500 hidden md:block"
                    style={{
                      animation: 'glitch-anim-2 2s infinite linear alternate',
                      clipPath: 'polygon(0 65%, 100% 65%, 100% 100%, 0 100%)',
                      transform: 'translateX(2px)'
                    }}
                  >
                    GLITCH EFFECT
                  </div>
                </>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        );
        
      default:
        return <div>Select an effect</div>;
    }
  };
  
  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 space-y-8">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Advanced UI Animation Effects</h1>
        
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-6">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('morph')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'morph' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Shape Morph
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('parallax')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'parallax' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Parallax Effect
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('stagger-reveal')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'stagger-reveal' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Staggered Reveal
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('fold-unfold')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'fold-unfold' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Fold/Unfold
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('blur-reveal')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'blur-reveal' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Blur Reveal
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('particle-reveal')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'particle-reveal' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Particle Reveal
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('swing-in')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'swing-in' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Swing In
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('shutter-reveal')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'shutter-reveal' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Shutter Reveal
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('glitch-text')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'glitch-text' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Glitch Effect
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mb-4">
          <button 
            onClick={triggerAnimation} 
            className="px-6 py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors"
          >
            Preview Animation
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="border border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-100 min-h-64">
          {renderEffect()}
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Current Effect: {activeEffect}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-700">
            {activeEffect === 'morph' && 'Element smoothly transforms from one shape to another while rotating. Great for state transitions.'}
            {activeEffect === 'parallax' && 'Different layers move at different speeds, creating depth. Often used in scrolling websites.'}
            {activeEffect === 'stagger-reveal' && 'Elements appear sequentially with a slight delay between each. Creates a choreographed entrance.'}
            {activeEffect === 'fold-unfold' && 'Content appears to unfold like a paper or card opening. Creates an elegant reveal.'}
            {activeEffect === 'blur-reveal' && 'Element transitions from blurry to sharp focus. Mimics camera focus and draws attention.'}
            {activeEffect === 'particle-reveal' && 'Content appears as particles scatter away. Creates a dramatic, explosive reveal effect.'}
            {activeEffect === 'swing-in' && 'Element swings into view as if attached to a pivot point. Adds natural motion physics.'}
            {activeEffect === 'shutter-reveal' && 'Content revealed by shutter-like panels sliding away. Similar to theatrical curtains opening.'}
            {activeEffect === 'glitch-text' && 'Text appears to glitch with color shifts and offsets. Creates a digital, distorted effect popular in tech/cyberpunk themes.'}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default AdvancedAnimationEffects;

import React, { useState } from 'react';

const AnimationEffects = () => {
  const [activeEffect, setActiveEffect] = useState('carousel');
  const [isAnimating, setIsAnimating] = useState(false);
  
  // Card data
  const cards = [
    { id: 1, color: 'bg-blue-500', title: 'Card 1' },
    { id: 2, color: 'bg-green-500', title: 'Card 2' },
    { id: 3, color: 'bg-yellow-500', title: 'Card 3' },
    { id: 4, color: 'bg-red-500', title: 'Card 4' },
    { id: 5, color: 'bg-purple-500', title: 'Card 5' }
  ];
  
  // Animation control
  const triggerAnimation = () => {
    setIsAnimating(true);
    setTimeout(() => setIsAnimating(false), 3000);
  };
  
  // Effect components
  const renderEffect = () => {
    switch(activeEffect) {
      case 'carousel':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full overflow-hidden">
            <div className={`flex transition-transform duration-3000 ease-in-out ${isAnimating ? 'transform -translate-x-full' : ''}`}>
              {cards.map(card => (
                <div key={card.id} className={`flex-shrink-0 w-64 h-48 mx-4 rounded-lg ${card.color} flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg`}>
                  {card.title}
                </div>
              ))}
              {cards.map(card => (
                <div key={`dup-${card.id}`} className={`flex-shrink-0 w-64 h-48 mx-4 rounded-lg ${card.color} flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg`}>
                  {card.title}
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'coverflow':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-80 w-full flex items-center justify-center perspective-1000">
            <div className="relative w-full flex justify-center items-center">
              {cards.map((card, index) => {
                // Calculate position and rotation based on index and animation state
                let position = index - 2; // Center the middle card
                if (isAnimating) {
                  position = (position + 1) % 5 - 2;
                }
                
                const translateX = position * 120;
                const rotateY = position * -15;
                const scale = 1 - Math.abs(position) * 0.15;
                const zIndex = 5 - Math.abs(position);
                
                return (
                  <div 
                    key={card.id} 
                    className={`absolute w-64 h-48 rounded-lg ${card.color} flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg transition-all duration-1000`}
                    style={{
                      transform: `translateX(${translateX}px) rotateY(${rotateY}deg) scale(${scale})`,
                      zIndex: zIndex,
                      opacity: scale
                    }}
                  >
                    {card.title}
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'fade-slide':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            {cards.slice(0, 3).map((card, index) => {
              // Calculate staggered positions and opacity for animation
              const baseDelay = index * 0.3;
              const translateX = isAnimating ? 0 : -100 + (index * 20);
              const opacity = isAnimating ? 1 : 0;
              
              return (
                <div 
                  key={card.id} 
                  className={`absolute w-64 h-48 rounded-lg ${card.color} flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg transition-all`}
                  style={{
                    transform: `translateX(${translateX}px)`,
                    opacity: opacity,
                    zIndex: index,
                    left: `${index * 20}px`,
                    transitionDelay: `${baseDelay}s`,
                    transitionDuration: '1s'
                  }}
                >
                  {card.title}
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'stack-slide':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            {cards.slice(0, 3).map((card, index) => {
              // Determine card position in stack
              let translateX, translateY, rotate, zIndex;
              
              if (isAnimating) {
                // Animated state (cards fanned out)
                translateX = (index - 1) * 100;
                translateY = 0;
                rotate = (index - 1) * 5;
                zIndex = 5 - index;
              } else {
                // Default state (cards stacked)
                translateX = 0;
                translateY = index * 5;
                rotate = 0;
                zIndex = 5 - index;
              }
              
              return (
                <div 
                  key={card.id} 
                  className={`absolute w-64 h-48 rounded-lg ${card.color} flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg transition-all duration-1000`}
                  style={{
                    transform: `translateX(${translateX}px) translateY(${translateY}px) rotate(${rotate}deg)`,
                    zIndex: zIndex
                  }}
                >
                  {card.title}
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        );

      case 'flip-card':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <div 
              className="w-64 h-48 relative preserve-3d transition-all duration-1000"
              style={{
                transform: isAnimating ? 'rotateY(180deg)' : 'rotateY(0deg)'
              }}
            >
              <div className={`absolute w-full h-full rounded-lg bg-blue-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg backface-hidden`}>
                Front Side
              </div>
              <div 
                className={`absolute w-full h-full rounded-lg bg-red-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg backface-hidden`}
                style={{ transform: 'rotateY(180deg)' }}
              >
                Back Side
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'scale-fade':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            {cards.slice(0, 3).map((card, index) => {
              const baseDelay = index * 0.2;
              const scale = isAnimating ? 1 : 0.5;
              const opacity = isAnimating ? 1 : 0;
              
              return (
                <div 
                  key={card.id} 
                  className={`absolute w-64 h-48 rounded-lg ${card.color} flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg transition-all`}
                  style={{
                    transform: `scale(${scale})`,
                    opacity: opacity,
                    zIndex: index,
                    left: `${index * 20}px`,
                    transitionDelay: `${baseDelay}s`,
                    transitionDuration: '0.8s'
                  }}
                >
                  {card.title}
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        );

      case 'accordion':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center">
            {cards.slice(0, 4).map((card, index) => {
              // Calculate height based on whether item is expanded
              const height = isAnimating && index === 1 ? '100px' : '40px';
              
              return (
                <div 
                  key={card.id} 
                  className={`w-full rounded-lg ${card.color} flex items-center px-4 shadow-md transition-all duration-700 overflow-hidden mb-2`}
                  style={{
                    height: height
                  }}
                >
                  <div className="font-bold text-white">{card.title}</div>
                  {isAnimating && index === 1 && (
                    <div className="ml-4 text-white mt-6">
                      Expanded content that appears when the accordion item is opened.
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        );

      case 'slide-drawer':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-start justify-start overflow-hidden">
            <div className="w-full h-full bg-gray-200 flex items-center justify-center">
              Main Content Area
            </div>
            <div 
              className="absolute top-0 left-0 h-full w-64 bg-blue-600 text-white p-4 transition-transform duration-500 transform shadow-lg"
              style={{
                transform: isAnimating ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(-100%)'
              }}
            >
              <div className="text-lg font-bold mb-4">Slide-in Drawer</div>
              <div>Navigation links or other content would appear here</div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      case 'elastic-motion':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <div 
              className="w-64 h-48 rounded-lg bg-purple-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg transition-all duration-1000"
              style={{
                transform: isAnimating ? 'translateX(100px) scale(1.1)' : 'translateX(0) scale(1)',
                transitionTimingFunction: 'cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.55, 0.265, 1.55)'
              }}
            >
              Elastic Motion
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      default:
        return <div>Select an effect</div>;
    }
  };
  
  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 space-y-8">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">UI Animation Effects Preview</h1>
        
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-6">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('carousel')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'carousel' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Scrolling/Sliding
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('coverflow')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'coverflow' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Cover Flow
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('fade-slide')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'fade-slide' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Fade & Slide
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('stack-slide')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'stack-slide' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Stack & Fan
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('flip-card')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'flip-card' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Card Flip
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('scale-fade')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'scale-fade' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Scale & Fade
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('accordion')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'accordion' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Accordion
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('slide-drawer')}
