            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'slide-drawer' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Slide Drawer
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('elastic-motion')} 
            className={`px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm ${activeEffect === 'elastic-motion' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Elastic Motion
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mb-4">
          <button 
            onClick={triggerAnimation} 
            className="px-6 py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors"
          >
            Preview Animation
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="border border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-100 min-h-64">
          {renderEffect()}
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Current Effect: {activeEffect}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-700">
            {activeEffect === 'carousel' && 'Horizontal scrolling/sliding of cards in sequence. Often used in carousels and image galleries.'}
            {activeEffect === 'coverflow' && 'Cards arranged in 3D space with perspective, rotation, and layering effects. Cards spin as they move positions.'}
            {activeEffect === 'fade-slide' && 'Cards fade in while sliding into position, creating a smooth entrance effect.'}
            {activeEffect === 'stack-slide' && 'Cards stacked on top of each other that fan out when animated.'}
            {activeEffect === 'flip-card' && '3D card flip effect that reveals content on the back side. Commonly used for revealing additional information.'}
            {activeEffect === 'scale-fade' && 'Cards scale up in size while fading in. Creates a smooth, attention-grabbing entrance.'}
            {activeEffect === 'accordion' && 'Vertical expanding/collapsing panels. Used for hierarchical content or FAQ sections.'}
            {activeEffect === 'slide-drawer' && 'Sliding panel that reveals from the edge of the screen. Common for navigation menus.'}
            {activeEffect === 'elastic-motion' && 'Animation with "springy" physics that overshoots then settles. Adds personality and organic feel.'}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default AnimationEffects;

import React, { useState } from 'react';

const AnimationEffects = () => {
  const [activeEffect, setActiveEffect] = useState('carousel');
  const [isAnimating, setIsAnimating] = useState(false);
  
  // Card data
  const cards = [
    { id: 1, color: 'bg-blue-500', title: 'Card 1' },
    { id: 2, color: 'bg-green-500', title: 'Card 2' },
    { id: 3, color: 'bg-yellow-500', title: 'Card 3' },
    { id: 4, color: 'bg-red-500', title: 'Card 4' },
    { id: 5, color: 'bg-purple-500', title: 'Card 5' }
  ];
  
  // Animation control
  const triggerAnimation = () => {
    setIsAnimating(true);
    setTimeout(() => setIsAnimating(false), 3000);
  };
  
  // Effect components
  const renderEffect = () => {
    switch(activeEffect) {
      case 'carousel':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full overflow-hidden">
            <div className={`flex transition-transform duration-3000 ease-in-out ${isAnimating ? 'transform -translate-x-full' : ''}`}>
              {cards.map(card => (
                <div key={card.id} className={`flex-shrink-0 w-64 h-48 mx-4 rounded-lg ${card.color} flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg`}>
                  {card.title}
                </div>
              ))}
              {cards.map(card => (
                <div key={`dup-${card.id}`} className={`flex-shrink-0 w-64 h-48 mx-4 rounded-lg ${card.color} flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg`}>
                  {card.title}
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'coverflow':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-80 w-full flex items-center justify-center perspective-1000">
            <div className="relative w-full flex justify-center items-center">
              {cards.map((card, index) => {
                // Calculate position and rotation based on index and animation state
                let position = index - 2; // Center the middle card
                if (isAnimating) {
                  position = (position + 1) % 5 - 2;
                }
                
                const translateX = position * 120;
                const rotateY = position * -15;
                const scale = 1 - Math.abs(position) * 0.15;
                const zIndex = 5 - Math.abs(position);
                
                return (
                  <div 
                    key={card.id} 
                    className={`absolute w-64 h-48 rounded-lg ${card.color} flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg transition-all duration-1000`}
                    style={{
                      transform: `translateX(${translateX}px) rotateY(${rotateY}deg) scale(${scale})`,
                      zIndex: zIndex,
                      opacity: scale
                    }}
                  >
                    {card.title}
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'fade-slide':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center">
            {cards.slice(0, 3).map((card, index) => {
              // Calculate staggered positions and opacity for animation
              const baseDelay = index * 0.3;
              const translateX = isAnimating ? 0 : -100 + (index * 20);
              const opacity = isAnimating ? 1 : 0;
              
              return (
                <div 
                  key={card.id} 
                  className={`absolute w-64 h-48 rounded-lg ${card.color} flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg transition-all`}
                  style={{
                    transform: `translateX(${translateX}px)`,
                    opacity: opacity,
                    zIndex: index,
                    left: `${index * 20}px`,
                    transitionDelay: `${baseDelay}s`,
                    transitionDuration: '1s'
                  }}
                >
                  {card.title}
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        );
        
      case 'stack-slide':
        return (
          <div className="relative h-64 w-full flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
            {cards.slice(0, 3).map((card, index) => {
              // Determine card position in stack
              let translateX, translateY, rotate, zIndex;
              
              if (isAnimating) {
                // Animated state (cards fanned out)
                translateX = (index - 1) * 100;
                translateY = 0;
                rotate = (index - 1) * 5;
                zIndex = 5 - index;
              } else {
                // Default state (cards stacked)
                translateX = 0;
                translateY = index * 5;
                rotate = 0;
                zIndex = 5 - index;
              }
              
              return (
                <div 
                  key={card.id} 
                  className={`absolute w-64 h-48 rounded-lg ${card.color} flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xl font-bold shadow-lg transition-all duration-1000`}
                  style={{
                    transform: `translateX(${translateX}px) translateY(${translateY}px) rotate(${rotate}deg)`,
                    zIndex: zIndex
                  }}
                >
                  {card.title}
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        );
        
      default:
        return <div>Select an effect</div>;
    }
  };
  
  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 space-y-8">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">UI Animation Effects Preview</h1>
        
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-6">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('carousel')} 
            className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-md ${activeEffect === 'carousel' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Scrolling/Sliding Across
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('coverflow')} 
            className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-md ${activeEffect === 'coverflow' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Cover Flow (Spin Effect)
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('fade-slide')} 
            className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-md ${activeEffect === 'fade-slide' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Fade and Slide In
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setActiveEffect('stack-slide')} 
            className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-md ${activeEffect === 'stack-slide' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200'}`}
          >
            Stack and Fan Out
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mb-4">
          <button 
            onClick={triggerAnimation} 
            className="px-6 py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors"
          >
            Preview Animation
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="border border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-100 min-h-64">
          {renderEffect()}
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Current Effect: {activeEffect}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-700">
            {activeEffect === 'carousel' && 'Horizontal scrolling/sliding of cards in sequence. Often used in carousels and image galleries.'}
            {activeEffect === 'coverflow' && 'Cards arranged in 3D space with perspective, rotation, and layering effects. Cards spin as they move positions.'}
            {activeEffect === 'fade-slide' && 'Cards fade in while sliding into position, creating a smooth entrance effect.'}
            {activeEffect === 'stack-slide' && 'Cards stacked on top of each other that fan out when animated.'}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default AnimationEffects;
